### ğŸ“… ç¬¬3å‘¨ï¼šè·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’åŠŸèƒ½å¼€å‘

#### ğŸ›£ï¸ æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½å®ç°

**1. è·¯å¾„è§„åˆ’APIé›†æˆ**

- **æŠ€æœ¯é€‰å‹**ï¼šOpenRouteService API æˆ– Mapbox Directions API
- **åŠŸèƒ½èŒƒå›´**ï¼šç‚¹å¯¹ç‚¹è·¯å¾„è§„åˆ’ã€å¤šç‚¹è·¯å¾„ä¼˜åŒ–ã€ä¸åŒäº¤é€šæ–¹å¼æ”¯æŒ

**2. è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’ç»„ä»¶å¼€å‘**

åˆ›å»º `RouteManager.vue` ç»„ä»¶ï¼š

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/Route/RouteManager.vue
<template>
  <div class="route-manager">
    <div class="route-controls mb-4">
      <el-button @click="planRoute" type="primary" :loading="isPlanning">
        ğŸ—ºï¸ è§„åˆ’è·¯çº¿
      </el-button>
      <el-button @click="optimizeRoute" :disabled="!hasRoute">
        âš¡ ä¼˜åŒ–è·¯çº¿
      </el-button>
      <el-button @click="clearRoute" :disabled="!hasRoute">
        ğŸ—‘ï¸ æ¸…é™¤è·¯çº¿
      </el-button>
    </div>
    
    <div class="route-options">
      <el-select v-model="transportMode" placeholder="é€‰æ‹©äº¤é€šæ–¹å¼">
        <el-option label="æ­¥è¡Œ" value="foot-walking" />
        <el-option label="é©¾è½¦" value="driving-car" />
        <el-option label="éª‘è¡Œ" value="cycling-regular" />
        <el-option label="å…¬å…±äº¤é€š" value="public-transport" />
      </el-select>
    </div>
    
    <div v-if="routeInfo" class="route-info mt-4">
      <h4>è·¯çº¿ä¿¡æ¯</h4>
      <p>æ€»è·ç¦»ï¼š{{ routeInfo.distance }}km</p>
      <p>é¢„è®¡æ—¶é—´ï¼š{{ routeInfo.duration }}åˆ†é’Ÿ</p>
      <p>é€”ç»ç‚¹æ•°ï¼š{{ routeInfo.waypoints }}ä¸ª</p>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
import { useMapStore } from '../../stores/map'
import { useRouteStore } from '../../stores/route'

const mapStore = useMapStore()
const routeStore = useRouteStore()

const isPlanning = ref(false)
const transportMode = ref('driving-car')

const hasRoute = computed(() => routeStore.currentRoute !== null)
const routeInfo = computed(() => routeStore.routeInfo)

const planRoute = async () => {
  if (mapStore.locations.length < 2) {
    ElMessage.warning('è‡³å°‘éœ€è¦2ä¸ªä½ç½®ç‚¹æ‰èƒ½è§„åˆ’è·¯çº¿')
    return
  }
  
  isPlanning.value = true
  try {
    await routeStore.planRoute(mapStore.locations, transportMode.value)
    ElMessage.success('è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’å®Œæˆ')
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’å¤±è´¥')
  } finally {
    isPlanning.value = false
  }
}

const optimizeRoute = async () => {
  await routeStore.optimizeRoute()
}

const clearRoute = () => {
  routeStore.clearRoute()
}
</script>
```

**3. è·¯çº¿çŠ¶æ€ç®¡ç†**

åˆ›å»º `route.ts` storeï¼š

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/stores/route.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia'
import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
import type { Location } from './map'

export interface RouteSegment {
  start: Location
  end: Location
  distance: number
  duration: number
  geometry: number[][]
}

export interface RouteInfo {
  totalDistance: number
  totalDuration: number
  segments: RouteSegment[]
  waypoints: Location[]
  transportMode: string
}

export const useRouteStore = defineStore('route', () => {
  const currentRoute = ref<RouteInfo | null>(null)
  const routeHistory = ref<RouteInfo[]>([])
  const isOptimizing = ref(false)
  
  const routeInfo = computed(() => {
    if (!currentRoute.value) return null
    return {
      distance: (currentRoute.value.totalDistance / 1000).toFixed(1),
      duration: Math.round(currentRoute.value.totalDuration / 60),
      waypoints: currentRoute.value.waypoints.length
    }
  })
  
  const planRoute = async (locations: Location[], mode: string) => {
    // è°ƒç”¨è·¯å¾„è§„åˆ’API
    const response = await fetch('/api/route/plan', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ locations, mode })
    })
    
    const routeData = await response.json()
    currentRoute.value = routeData
    routeHistory.value.push(routeData)
  }
  
  const optimizeRoute = async () => {
    if (!currentRoute.value) return
    
    isOptimizing.value = true
    try {
      // ä½¿ç”¨TSPç®—æ³•ä¼˜åŒ–è·¯å¾„
      const optimized = await optimizeTSP(currentRoute.value.waypoints)
      await planRoute(optimized, currentRoute.value.transportMode)
    } finally {
      isOptimizing.value = false
    }
  }
  
  const clearRoute = () => {
    currentRoute.value = null
  }
  
  return {
    currentRoute,
    routeHistory,
    isOptimizing,
    routeInfo,
    planRoute,
    optimizeRoute,
    clearRoute
  }
})
```

- åˆ›å»ºè·¯çº¿ç›¸å…³çš„ç±»å‹å®šä¹‰

**1. æœ¬åœ°å­˜å‚¨ç®¡ç†**

åˆ›å»º `DataManager.vue` ç»„ä»¶ï¼š

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/Data/DataManager.vue
<template>
  <div class="data-manager">
    <el-card class="mb-4">
      <template #header>
        <span>ğŸ“Š æ•°æ®ç®¡ç†</span>
      </template>
      
      <div class="data-actions space-y-3">
        <div class="export-section">
          <h4>å¯¼å‡ºæ•°æ®</h4>
          <el-button-group>
            <el-button @click="exportJSON" icon="Download">
              å¯¼å‡ºJSON
            </el-button>
            <el-button @click="exportGPX" icon="Download">
              å¯¼å‡ºGPX
            </el-button>
            <el-button @click="exportKML" icon="Download">
              å¯¼å‡ºKML
            </el-button>
          </el-button-group>
        </div>
        
        <div class="import-section">
          <h4>å¯¼å…¥æ•°æ®</h4>
          <el-upload
            :before-upload="handleImport"
            :show-file-list="false"
            accept=".json,.gpx,.kml"
          >
            <el-button icon="Upload">é€‰æ‹©æ–‡ä»¶å¯¼å…¥</el-button>
          </el-upload>
        </div>
        
        <div class="sync-section">
          <h4>äº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥</h4>
          <el-button @click="syncToCloud" :loading="isSyncing">
            â˜ï¸ åŒæ­¥åˆ°äº‘ç«¯
          </el-button>
          <el-button @click="loadFromCloud">
            ğŸ“¥ ä»äº‘ç«¯åŠ è½½
          </el-button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </el-card>
    
    <el-card>
      <template #header>
        <span>ğŸ“ˆ æ•°æ®ç»Ÿè®¡</span>
      </template>
      
      <div class="stats-grid grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <div class="stat-item">
          <div class="stat-value">{{ totalLocations }}</div>
          <div class="stat-label">æ€»ä½ç½®æ•°</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-item">
          <div class="stat-value">{{ totalRoutes }}</div>
          <div class="stat-label">è·¯çº¿æ•°é‡</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-item">
          <div class="stat-value">{{ totalDistance }}km</div>
          <div class="stat-label">æ€»è·ç¦»</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-item">
          <div class="stat-value">{{ storageUsed }}MB</div>
          <div class="stat-label">å­˜å‚¨ä½¿ç”¨</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </el-card>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
import { useDataStore } from '../../stores/data'
import { useMapStore } from '../../stores/map'
import { useRouteStore } from '../../stores/route'

const dataStore = useDataStore()
const mapStore = useMapStore()
const routeStore = useRouteStore()

const isSyncing = ref(false)

const totalLocations = computed(() => mapStore.totalLocations)
const totalRoutes = computed(() => routeStore.routeHistory.length)
const totalDistance = computed(() => dataStore.calculateTotalDistance())
const storageUsed = computed(() => dataStore.getStorageUsage())

const exportJSON = () => {
  dataStore.exportData('json')
}

const exportGPX = () => {
  dataStore.exportData('gpx')
}

const exportKML = () => {
  dataStore.exportData('kml')
}

const handleImport = (file: File) => {
  dataStore.importData(file)
  return false // é˜»æ­¢è‡ªåŠ¨ä¸Šä¼ 
}

const syncToCloud = async () => {
  isSyncing.value = true
  try {
    await dataStore.syncToCloud()
    ElMessage.success('åŒæ­¥æˆåŠŸ')
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('åŒæ­¥å¤±è´¥')
  } finally {
    isSyncing.value = false
  }
}

const loadFromCloud = async () => {
  await dataStore.loadFromCloud()
}
```

**2. æ•°æ®å­˜å‚¨Store**

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/stores/data.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia'
import { ref } from 'vue'
import { useMapStore } from './map'
import { useRouteStore } from './route'

export const useDataStore = defineStore('data', () => {
  const lastSyncTime = ref<Date | null>(null)
  const autoSaveEnabled = ref(true)
  
  // å¯¼å‡ºæ•°æ®
  const exportData = (format: 'json' | 'gpx' | 'kml') => {
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    const routeStore = useRouteStore()
    
    const data = {
      locations: mapStore.locations,
      routes: routeStore.routeHistory,
      exportTime: new Date().toISOString(),
      version: '1.0.0'
    }
    
    let content: string
    let filename: string
    let mimeType: string
    
    switch (format) {
      case 'json':
        content = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${Date.now()}.json`
        mimeType = 'application/json'
        break
      case 'gpx':
        content = convertToGPX(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${Date.now()}.gpx`
        mimeType = 'application/gpx+xml'
        break
      case 'kml':
        content = convertToKML(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${Date.now()}.kml`
        mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-earth.kml+xml'
        break
    }
    
    downloadFile(content, filename, mimeType)
  }
  
  // å¯¼å…¥æ•°æ®
  const importData = async (file: File) => {
    const text = await file.text()
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    const routeStore = useRouteStore()
    
    try {
      if (file.name.endsWith('.json')) {
        const data = JSON.parse(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations || []
        routeStore.routeHistory = data.routes || []
      } else if (file.name.endsWith('.gpx')) {
        const data = parseGPX(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations
      } else if (file.name.endsWith('.kml')) {
        const data = parseKML(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations
      }
      
      ElMessage.success('æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥æˆåŠŸ')
    } catch (error) {
      ElMessage.error('æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥å¤±è´¥')
    }
  }
  
  // äº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥
  const syncToCloud = async () => {
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    const routeStore = useRouteStore()
    
    const data = {
      locations: mapStore.locations,
      routes: routeStore.routeHistory,
      syncTime: new Date().toISOString()
    }
    
    // è¿™é‡Œå¯ä»¥é›†æˆFirebaseã€Supabaseç­‰äº‘æœåŠ¡
    await fetch('/api/sync/upload', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(data)
    })
    
    lastSyncTime.value = new Date()
  }
  
  const loadFromCloud = async () => {
    const response = await fetch('/api/sync/download')
    const data = await response.json()
    
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    const routeStore = useRouteStore()
    
    mapStore.locations = data.locations || []
    routeStore.routeHistory = data.routes || []
  }
  
  return {
    lastSyncTime,
    autoSaveEnabled,
    exportData,
    importData,
    syncToCloud,
    loadFromCloud
  }
})
```

### ğŸ› ï¸ GPXè§£æå™¨ç±»å‹å®šä¹‰

ç”±äº `gpx-parser` æ²¡æœ‰å®˜æ–¹ç±»å‹å®šä¹‰ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬éœ€è¦åˆ›å»ºè‡ªå®šä¹‰ç±»å‹ï¼š

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/types/gpx.d.ts
declare module 'gpx-parser' {
  export interface GPXTrack {
    name: string;
    segments: GPXTrackSegment[];
  }
  
  export interface GPXTrackSegment {
    points: GPXPoint[];
  }
  
  export interface GPXPoint {
    lat: number;
    lon: number;
    ele?: number;
    time?: Date;
  }
  
  export interface GPXWaypoint {
    name: string;
    lat: number;
    lon: number;
    ele?: number;
    desc?: string;
  }
  
  export interface GPXData {
    tracks: GPXTrack[];
    waypoints: GPXWaypoint[];
    routes: any[];
    metadata: {
      name?: string;
      desc?: string;
      time?: Date;
    };
  }
  
  export function parse(gpxString: string): GPXData;
}
```

### ğŸ”„ æ›´æ–°æ•°æ®å­˜å‚¨Store

ç°åœ¨å¯ä»¥æ­£ç¡®å®ç° <mcfile name="data.ts" path="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/stores/data.ts"></mcfile>ï¼š

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/stores/data.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia'
import { ref } from 'vue'
import { useMapStore } from './map'
import * as gpxParser from 'gpx-parser'
import { parseString } from 'xml2js'
import type { Location } from './map'

export const useDataStore = defineStore('data', () => {
  const lastSyncTime = ref<Date | null>(null)
  const autoSaveEnabled = ref(true)
  
  // å¯¼å‡ºä¸ºGPXæ ¼å¼
  const convertToGPX = (data: any): string => {
    const locations = data.locations as Location[]
    
    let gpxContent = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<gpx version="1.1" creator="MAPSXPLR">
  <metadata>
    <name>MAPSXPLR Export</name>
    <time>${new Date().toISOString()}</time>
  </metadata>
`
    
    // æ·»åŠ èˆªç‚¹
    locations.forEach(location => {
      gpxContent += `  <wpt lat="${location.coordinates[0]}" lon="${location.coordinates[1]}">
`
      gpxContent += `    <name>${location.name}</name>
`
      if (location.description) {
        gpxContent += `    <desc>${location.description}</desc>
`
      }
      gpxContent += `  </wpt>
`
    })
    
    gpxContent += `</gpx>`
    return gpxContent
  }
  
  // è§£æGPXæ–‡ä»¶
  const parseGPX = (gpxString: string): { locations: Location[] } => {
    try {
      const gpxData = gpxParser.parse(gpxString)
      const locations: Location[] = []
      
      // è§£æèˆªç‚¹
      gpxData.waypoints.forEach((waypoint, index) => {
        locations.push({
          id: Date.now() + index,
          name: waypoint.name || `ä½ç½® ${index + 1}`,
          coordinates: [waypoint.lat, waypoint.lon],
          description: waypoint.desc,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        })
      })
      
      // è§£æè½¨è¿¹ç‚¹
      gpxData.tracks.forEach(track => {
        track.segments.forEach(segment => {
          segment.points.forEach((point, index) => {
            locations.push({
              id: Date.now() + locations.length + index,
              name: `è½¨è¿¹ç‚¹ ${index + 1}`,
              coordinates: [point.lat, point.lon],
              timestamp: point.time?.toISOString() || new Date().toISOString()
            })
          })
        })
      })
      
      return { locations }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('GPXè§£æå¤±è´¥:', error)
      throw new Error('GPXæ–‡ä»¶æ ¼å¼ä¸æ­£ç¡®')
    }
  }
  
  // å¯¼å‡ºä¸ºKMLæ ¼å¼
  const convertToKML = (data: any): string => {
    const locations = data.locations as Location[]
    
    let kmlContent = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<kml xmlns="http://www.opengis.net/kml/2.2">
  <Document>
    <name>MAPSXPLR Export</name>
`
    
    locations.forEach(location => {
      kmlContent += `    <Placemark>
`
      kmlContent += `      <name>${location.name}</name>
`
      if (location.description) {
        kmlContent += `      <description>${location.description}</description>
`
      }
      kmlContent += `      <Point>
`
      kmlContent += `        <coordinates>${location.coordinates[1]},${location.coordinates[0]},0</coordinates>
`
      kmlContent += `      </Point>
`
      kmlContent += `    </Placemark>
`
    })
    
    kmlContent += `  </Document>
</kml>`
    return kmlContent
  }
  
  // è§£æKMLæ–‡ä»¶
  const parseKML = async (kmlString: string): Promise<{ locations: Location[] }> => {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      parseString(kmlString, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
          reject(new Error('KMLæ–‡ä»¶è§£æå¤±è´¥'))
          return
        }
        
        const locations: Location[] = []
        const placemarks = result?.kml?.Document?.[0]?.Placemark || []
        
        placemarks.forEach((placemark: any, index: number) => {
          const coordinates = placemark.Point?.[0]?.coordinates?.[0]
          if (coordinates) {
            const [lon, lat] = coordinates.split(',').map(Number)
            locations.push({
              id: Date.now() + index,
              name: placemark.name?.[0] || `ä½ç½® ${index + 1}`,
              coordinates: [lat, lon],
              description: placemark.description?.[0],
              timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            })
          }
        })
        
        resolve({ locations })
      })
    })
  }
  
  // ä¸‹è½½æ–‡ä»¶è¾…åŠ©å‡½æ•°
  const downloadFile = (content: string, filename: string, mimeType: string) => {
    const blob = new Blob([content], { type: mimeType })
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
    const link = document.createElement('a')
    link.href = url
    link.download = filename
    document.body.appendChild(link)
    link.click()
    document.body.removeChild(link)
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url)
  }
  
  // å¯¼å‡ºæ•°æ®
  const exportData = (format: 'json' | 'gpx' | 'kml') => {
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    
    const data = {
      locations: mapStore.locations,
      exportTime: new Date().toISOString(),
      version: '1.0.0'
    }
    
    let content: string
    let filename: string
    let mimeType: string
    
    switch (format) {
      case 'json':
        content = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${Date.now()}.json`
        mimeType = 'application/json'
        break
      case 'gpx':
        content = convertToGPX(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${Date.now()}.gpx`
        mimeType = 'application/gpx+xml'
        break
      case 'kml':
        content = convertToKML(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${Date.now()}.kml`
        mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-earth.kml+xml'
        break
    }
    
    downloadFile(content, filename, mimeType)
  }
  
  // å¯¼å…¥æ•°æ®
  const importData = async (file: File) => {
    const text = await file.text()
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    
    try {
      if (file.name.endsWith('.json')) {
        const data = JSON.parse(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations || []
      } else if (file.name.endsWith('.gpx')) {
        const data = parseGPX(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations
      } else if (file.name.endsWith('.kml')) {
        const data = await parseKML(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations
      }
      
      return true
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥å¤±è´¥:', error)
      throw error
    }
  }
  
  return {
    lastSyncTime,
    autoSaveEnabled,
    exportData,
    importData,
    convertToGPX,
    convertToKML,
    parseGPX,
    parseKML
  }
})
```

### ğŸ› ï¸ æ›´æ–°æ•°æ®å­˜å‚¨Store

ä½¿ç”¨ `@tmcw/togeojson` çš„å®Œæ•´å®ç°ï¼š

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/stores/data.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia'
import { ref } from 'vue'
import { useMapStore } from './map'
import * as toGeoJSON from '@tmcw/togeojson'
import { parseString } from 'xml2js'
import type { Location } from './map'

export const useDataStore = defineStore('data', () => {
  const lastSyncTime = ref<Date | null>(null)
  const autoSaveEnabled = ref(true)
  
  // å¯¼å‡ºä¸ºGPXæ ¼å¼
  const convertToGPX = (data: any): string => {
    const locations = data.locations as Location[]
    
    let gpxContent = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<gpx version="1.1" creator="MAPSXPLR" xmlns="http://www.topografix.com/GPX/1/1">
  <metadata>
    <name>MAPSXPLR Export</name>
    <time>${new Date().toISOString()}</time>
  </metadata>
`
    
    // æ·»åŠ èˆªç‚¹
    locations.forEach(location => {
      gpxContent += `  <wpt lat="${location.coordinates[0]}" lon="${location.coordinates[1]}">
`
      gpxContent += `    <name><![CDATA[${location.name}]]></name>
`
      if (location.description) {
        gpxContent += `    <desc><![CDATA[${location.description}]]></desc>
`
      }
      if (location.category) {
        gpxContent += `    <type>${location.category}</type>
`
      }
      gpxContent += `    <time>${location.timestamp}</time>
`
      gpxContent += `  </wpt>
`
    })
    
    gpxContent += `</gpx>`
    return gpxContent
  }
  
  // è§£æGPXæ–‡ä»¶ï¼ˆä½¿ç”¨toGeoJSONï¼‰
  const parseGPX = (gpxString: string): { locations: Location[] } => {
    try {
      // åˆ›å»ºDOMè§£æå™¨
      const parser = new DOMParser()
      const gpxDoc = parser.parseFromString(gpxString, 'text/xml')
      
      // è½¬æ¢ä¸ºGeoJSON
      const geoJSON = toGeoJSON.gpx(gpxDoc)
      const locations: Location[] = []
      
      // è§£æç‰¹å¾ç‚¹
      geoJSON.features.forEach((feature, index) => {
        if (feature.geometry.type === 'Point') {
          const [lon, lat] = feature.geometry.coordinates
          locations.push({
            id: Date.now() + index,
            name: feature.properties?.name || `ä½ç½® ${index + 1}`,
            coordinates: [lat, lon],
            description: feature.properties?.desc || feature.properties?.description,
            timestamp: feature.properties?.time || new Date().toISOString(),
            category: feature.properties?.type
          })
        } else if (feature.geometry.type === 'LineString') {
          // å¤„ç†è½¨è¿¹çº¿
          feature.geometry.coordinates.forEach((coord, coordIndex) => {
            const [lon, lat] = coord
            locations.push({
              id: Date.now() + locations.length + coordIndex,
              name: `è½¨è¿¹ç‚¹ ${coordIndex + 1}`,
              coordinates: [lat, lon],
              timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            })
          })
        }
      })
      
      return { locations }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('GPXè§£æå¤±è´¥:', error)
      throw new Error('GPXæ–‡ä»¶æ ¼å¼ä¸æ­£ç¡®')
    }
  }
  
  // è‡ªå®šä¹‰GPXè§£æå™¨ï¼ˆå¤‡ç”¨æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼‰
  const parseGPXCustom = async (gpxString: string): Promise<{ locations: Location[] }> => {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      parseString(gpxString, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
          reject(new Error('GPXæ–‡ä»¶è§£æå¤±è´¥'))
          return
        }
        
        const locations: Location[] = []
        
        try {
          // è§£æèˆªç‚¹
          const waypoints = result?.gpx?.wpt || []
          waypoints.forEach((wpt: any, index: number) => {
            locations.push({
              id: Date.now() + index,
              name: wpt.name?.[0] || `èˆªç‚¹ ${index + 1}`,
              coordinates: [parseFloat(wpt.$.lat), parseFloat(wpt.$.lon)],
              description: wpt.desc?.[0],
              timestamp: wpt.time?.[0] || new Date().toISOString(),
              category: wpt.type?.[0]
            })
          })
          
          // è§£æè½¨è¿¹
          const tracks = result?.gpx?.trk || []
          tracks.forEach((track: any) => {
            const segments = track.trkseg || []
            segments.forEach((segment: any) => {
              const points = segment.trkpt || []
              points.forEach((point: any, index: number) => {
                locations.push({
                  id: Date.now() + locations.length + index,
                  name: `è½¨è¿¹ç‚¹ ${index + 1}`,
                  coordinates: [parseFloat(point.$.lat), parseFloat(point.$.lon)],
                  timestamp: point.time?.[0] || new Date().toISOString()
                })
              })
            })
          })
          
          resolve({ locations })
        } catch (parseError) {
          reject(new Error('GPXæ•°æ®è§£æå¤±è´¥'))
        }
      })
    })
  }
  
  // å¯¼å‡ºä¸ºKMLæ ¼å¼
  const convertToKML = (data: any): string => {
    const locations = data.locations as Location[]
    
    let kmlContent = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<kml xmlns="http://www.opengis.net/kml/2.2">
  <Document>
    <name>MAPSXPLR Export</name>
    <description>Exported from MAPSXPLR on ${new Date().toISOString()}</description>
`
    
    locations.forEach(location => {
      kmlContent += `    <Placemark>
`
      kmlContent += `      <name><![CDATA[${location.name}]]></name>
`
      if (location.description) {
        kmlContent += `      <description><![CDATA[${location.description}]]></description>
`
      }
      kmlContent += `      <TimeStamp><when>${location.timestamp}</when></TimeStamp>
`
      kmlContent += `      <Point>
`
      kmlContent += `        <coordinates>${location.coordinates[1]},${location.coordinates[0]},0</coordinates>
`
      kmlContent += `      </Point>
`
      kmlContent += `    </Placemark>
`
    })
    
    kmlContent += `  </Document>
</kml>`
    return kmlContent
  }
  
  // è§£æKMLæ–‡ä»¶
  const parseKML = async (kmlString: string): Promise<{ locations: Location[] }> => {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      parseString(kmlString, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
          reject(new Error('KMLæ–‡ä»¶è§£æå¤±è´¥'))
          return
        }
        
        const locations: Location[] = []
        
        try {
          const placemarks = result?.kml?.Document?.[0]?.Placemark || []
          
          placemarks.forEach((placemark: any, index: number) => {
            const coordinates = placemark.Point?.[0]?.coordinates?.[0]
            if (coordinates) {
              const [lon, lat, alt] = coordinates.split(',').map(Number)
              locations.push({
                id: Date.now() + index,
                name: placemark.name?.[0] || `ä½ç½® ${index + 1}`,
                coordinates: [lat, lon],
                description: placemark.description?.[0],
                timestamp: placemark.TimeStamp?.[0]?.when?.[0] || new Date().toISOString()
              })
            }
          })
          
          resolve({ locations })
        } catch (parseError) {
          reject(new Error('KMLæ•°æ®è§£æå¤±è´¥'))
        }
      })
    })
  }
  
  // ä¸‹è½½æ–‡ä»¶è¾…åŠ©å‡½æ•°
  const downloadFile = (content: string, filename: string, mimeType: string) => {
    const blob = new Blob([content], { type: mimeType })
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
    const link = document.createElement('a')
    link.href = url
    link.download = filename
    link.style.display = 'none'
    document.body.appendChild(link)
    link.click()
    document.body.removeChild(link)
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url)
  }
  
  // è®¡ç®—å­˜å‚¨ä½¿ç”¨é‡
  const getStorageUsage = (): string => {
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    const dataSize = JSON.stringify({
      locations: mapStore.locations
    }).length
    return (dataSize / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)
  }
  
  // è®¡ç®—æ€»è·ç¦»
  const calculateTotalDistance = (): string => {
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    let totalDistance = 0
    
    for (let i = 0; i < mapStore.locations.length - 1; i++) {
      const loc1 = mapStore.locations[i]
      const loc2 = mapStore.locations[i + 1]
      
      // ä½¿ç”¨Haversineå…¬å¼è®¡ç®—è·ç¦»
      const R = 6371 // åœ°çƒåŠå¾„ï¼ˆå…¬é‡Œï¼‰
      const dLat = (loc2.coordinates[0] - loc1.coordinates[0]) * Math.PI / 180
      const dLon = (loc2.coordinates[1] - loc1.coordinates[1]) * Math.PI / 180
      const a = Math.sin(dLat/2) * Math.sin(dLat/2) +
                Math.cos(loc1.coordinates[0] * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(loc2.coordinates[0] * Math.PI / 180) *
                Math.sin(dLon/2) * Math.sin(dLon/2)
      const c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1-a))
      totalDistance += R * c
    }
    
    return totalDistance.toFixed(1)
  }
  
  // å¯¼å‡ºæ•°æ®
  const exportData = (format: 'json' | 'gpx' | 'kml') => {
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    
    const data = {
      locations: mapStore.locations,
      exportTime: new Date().toISOString(),
      version: '1.0.0'
    }
    
    let content: string
    let filename: string
    let mimeType: string
    
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19).replace(/[:-]/g, '')
    
    switch (format) {
      case 'json':
        content = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${timestamp}.json`
        mimeType = 'application/json'
        break
      case 'gpx':
        content = convertToGPX(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${timestamp}.gpx`
        mimeType = 'application/gpx+xml'
        break
      case 'kml':
        content = convertToKML(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-data-${timestamp}.kml`
        mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-earth.kml+xml'
        break
    }
    
    downloadFile(content, filename, mimeType)
  }
  
  // å¯¼å…¥æ•°æ®
  const importData = async (file: File) => {
    const text = await file.text()
    const mapStore = useMapStore()
    
    try {
      if (file.name.endsWith('.json')) {
        const data = JSON.parse(text)
        if (data.locations && Array.isArray(data.locations)) {
          mapStore.locations = data.locations
        } else {
          throw new Error('JSONæ–‡ä»¶æ ¼å¼ä¸æ­£ç¡®')
        }
      } else if (file.name.endsWith('.gpx')) {
        const data = parseGPX(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations
      } else if (file.name.endsWith('.kml')) {
        const data = await parseKML(text)
        mapStore.locations = data.locations
      } else {
        throw new Error('ä¸æ”¯æŒçš„æ–‡ä»¶æ ¼å¼')
      }
      
      return true
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥å¤±è´¥:', error)
      throw error
    }
  }
  
  return {
    lastSyncTime,
    autoSaveEnabled,
    exportData,
    importData,
    convertToGPX,
    convertToKML,
    parseGPX,
    parseKML: parseKML,
    getStorageUsage,
    calculateTotalDistance
  }
})
```

### ğŸ¯ ç±»å‹å®šä¹‰æ–‡ä»¶

åˆ›å»º `src/types/gpx.d.ts`ï¼š

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/types/gpx.d.ts
// GPXç›¸å…³ç±»å‹å®šä¹‰
export interface GPXWaypoint {
  lat: number
  lon: number
  name?: string
  desc?: string
  type?: string
  time?: string
}

export interface GPXTrackPoint {
  lat: number
  lon: number
  ele?: number
  time?: string
}

export interface GPXTrackSegment {
  points: GPXTrackPoint[]
}

export interface GPXTrack {
  name?: string
  segments: GPXTrackSegment[]
}

export interface GPXData {
  waypoints: GPXWaypoint[]
  tracks: GPXTrack[]
  routes: any[]
  metadata?: {
    name?: string
    desc?: string
    time?: string
  }
}

// æ‰©å±•toGeoJSONæ¨¡å—ç±»å‹
declare module '@tmcw/togeojson' {
  export function gpx(doc: Document): GeoJSON.FeatureCollection
  export function kml(doc: Document): GeoJSON.FeatureCollection
}
```

### 3. åˆ›å»ºAIèŠå¤©ç»„ä»¶

é¦–å…ˆåˆ›å»ºèŠå¤©çŠ¶æ€ç®¡ç†ï¼š

```typescript:src/stores/chat.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia'
import { ref, computed } from 'vue'

export interface ChatMessage {
  id: string
  content: string
  role: 'user' | 'assistant'
  timestamp: Date
  type?: 'text' | 'location' | 'route'
}

export const useChatStore = defineStore('chat', () => {
  const messages = ref<ChatMessage[]>([])
  const isThinking = ref(false)
  const currentConversation = ref<string | null>(null)
  
  const lastMessage = computed(() => {
    return messages.value[messages.value.length - 1]
  })
  
  const addMessage = (content: string, role: 'user' | 'assistant', type: 'text' | 'location' | 'route' = 'text') => {
    const message: ChatMessage = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      content,
      role,
      timestamp: new Date(),
      type
    }
    messages.value.push(message)
  }
  
  const sendMessage = async (content: string) => {
    // æ·»åŠ ç”¨æˆ·æ¶ˆæ¯
    addMessage(content, 'user')
    isThinking.value = true
    
    try {
      // è°ƒç”¨AI API
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-chat', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          message: content,
          history: messages.value.slice(-10) // åªå‘é€æœ€è¿‘10æ¡æ¶ˆæ¯
        })
      })
      
      const data = await response.json()
      
      if (data.success) {
        addMessage(data.response, 'assistant')
        
        // å¦‚æœAIè¿”å›äº†ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯ï¼Œå¤„ç†ä½ç½®æ•°æ®
        if (data.locations) {
          // è¿™é‡Œå¯ä»¥è°ƒç”¨åœ°å›¾storeæ¥æ·»åŠ ä½ç½®
        }
      } else {
        addMessage('æŠ±æ­‰ï¼Œæˆ‘é‡åˆ°äº†ä¸€äº›é—®é¢˜ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åå†è¯•ã€‚', 'assistant')
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Chat error:', error)
      addMessage('ç½‘ç»œè¿æ¥å‡ºç°é—®é¢˜ï¼Œè¯·æ£€æŸ¥ç½‘ç»œåé‡è¯•ã€‚', 'assistant')
    } finally {
      isThinking.value = false
    }
  }
  
  const clearChat = () => {
    messages.value = []
    currentConversation.value = null
  }
  
  return {
    messages,
    isThinking,
    currentConversation,
    lastMessage,
    addMessage,
    sendMessage,
    clearChat
  }
})
```

### 4. åˆ›å»ºAIèŠå¤©ç»„ä»¶

```vue:src/components/Chat/AIChatBot.vue
<template>
  <div class="ai-chatbot h-96 flex flex-col">
    <!-- èŠå¤©æ¶ˆæ¯åŒºåŸŸ -->
    <div 
      ref="messagesContainer" 
      class="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-t-lg"
    >
      <div v-if="chatStore.messages.length === 0" class="text-center text-gray-500 py-8">
        <div class="text-4xl mb-2">ğŸ¤–</div>
        <p>ä½ å¥½ï¼æˆ‘æ˜¯ä½ çš„AIæ—…è¡ŒåŠ©æ‰‹</p>
        <p class="text-sm mt-1">ä½ å¯ä»¥é—®æˆ‘å…³äºåœ°ç‚¹æ¨èã€è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’ç­‰é—®é¢˜</p>
      </div>
      
      <div 
        v-for="message in chatStore.messages" 
        :key="message.id"
        :class="[
          'flex',
          message.role === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'
        ]"
      >
        <div 
          :class="[
            'max-w-xs lg:max-w-md px-4 py-2 rounded-lg',
            message.role === 'user' 
              ? 'bg-blue-500 text-white' 
              : 'bg-white text-gray-800 shadow-sm'
          ]"
        >
          <p class="text-sm">{{ message.content }}</p>
          <p class="text-xs mt-1 opacity-70">
            {{ formatTime(message.timestamp) }}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- AIæ€è€ƒä¸­çš„æç¤º -->
      <div v-if="chatStore.isThinking" class="flex justify-start">
        <div class="bg-white text-gray-800 shadow-sm px-4 py-2 rounded-lg">
          <div class="flex items-center space-x-2">
            <div class="animate-spin rounded-full h-4 w-4 border-b-2 border-blue-500"></div>
            <span class="text-sm">AIæ­£åœ¨æ€è€ƒ...</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- è¾“å…¥åŒºåŸŸ -->
    <div class="p-4 bg-white rounded-b-lg border-t">
      <div class="flex space-x-2">
        <el-input
          v-model="userInput"
          placeholder="è¯¢é—®AIå…³äºåœ°ç‚¹æ¨èã€è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’..."
          @keyup.enter="sendMessage"
          :disabled="chatStore.isThinking"
          class="flex-1"
        />
        <el-button 
          @click="sendMessage" 
          :loading="chatStore.isThinking"
          type="primary"
          icon="ChatDotRound"
        >
          å‘é€
        </el-button>
      </div>
      
      <!-- å¿«æ·æ“ä½œæŒ‰é’® -->
      <div class="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
        <el-button 
          size="small" 
          @click="quickAsk('æ¨èåŒ—äº¬çš„çƒ­é—¨æ™¯ç‚¹')"
          :disabled="chatStore.isThinking"
        >
          ğŸ›ï¸ æ¨èæ™¯ç‚¹
        </el-button>
        <el-button 
          size="small" 
          @click="quickAsk('å¸®æˆ‘è§„åˆ’ä¸€æ—¥æ¸¸è·¯çº¿')"
          :disabled="chatStore.isThinking"
        >
          ğŸ—ºï¸ è§„åˆ’è·¯çº¿
        </el-button>
        <el-button 
          size="small" 
          @click="quickAsk('é™„è¿‘æœ‰ä»€ä¹ˆå¥½åƒçš„é¤å…')"
          :disabled="chatStore.isThinking"
        >
          ğŸ½ï¸ æ‰¾ç¾é£Ÿ
        </el-button>
        <el-button 
          size="small" 
          @click="chatStore.clearChat()"
          :disabled="chatStore.isThinking"
        >
          ğŸ—‘ï¸ æ¸…ç©ºå¯¹è¯
        </el-button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, nextTick, onMounted } from 'vue'
import { ElInput, ElButton } from 'element-plus'
import { useChatStore } from '../../stores/chat'

const chatStore = useChatStore()
const userInput = ref('')
const messagesContainer = ref<HTMLElement>()

const formatTime = (date: Date) => {
  return date.toLocaleTimeString('zh-CN', { 
    hour: '2-digit', 
    minute: '2-digit' 
  })
}

const sendMessage = async () => {
  if (!userInput.value.trim() || chatStore.isThinking) return
  
  const message = userInput.value.trim()
  userInput.value = ''
  
  await chatStore.sendMessage(message)
  scrollToBottom()
}

const quickAsk = (question: string) => {
  userInput.value = question
  sendMessage()
}

const scrollToBottom = async () => {
  await nextTick()
  if (messagesContainer.value) {
    messagesContainer.value.scrollTop = messagesContainer.value.scrollHeight
  }
}

onMounted(() => {
  // æ·»åŠ æ¬¢è¿æ¶ˆæ¯
  if (chatStore.messages.length === 0) {
    chatStore.addMessage(
      'ä½ å¥½ï¼æˆ‘æ˜¯ä½ çš„AIæ—…è¡ŒåŠ©æ‰‹ã€‚æˆ‘å¯ä»¥å¸®ä½ æ¨èæ™¯ç‚¹ã€è§„åˆ’è·¯çº¿ã€å¯»æ‰¾ç¾é£Ÿç­‰ã€‚æœ‰ä»€ä¹ˆæˆ‘å¯ä»¥å¸®åŠ©ä½ çš„å—ï¼Ÿ',
      'assistant'
    )
  }
})
</script>
```

### 5. åˆ›å»ºAPIè·¯ç”±

```typescript:src/pages/api/ai-chat.ts
import type { APIRoute } from 'astro'

// è¿™é‡Œå¯ä»¥é…ç½®ä¸åŒçš„AIæœåŠ¡
const AI_CONFIG = {
  // ä½¿ç”¨DeepSeek API
  provider: 'deepseek',
  apiKey: process.env.DEEPSEEK_API_KEY || '',
  baseURL: 'https://api.deepseek.com/v1',
  model: 'deepseek-chat'
}

export const POST: APIRoute = async ({ request }) => {
  try {
    const { message, history } = await request.json()
    
    // æ„å»ºå¯¹è¯ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡
    const messages = [
      {
        role: 'system',
        content: `ä½ æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªä¸“ä¸šçš„æ—…è¡ŒåŠ©æ‰‹AIï¼Œä¸“é—¨å¸®åŠ©ç”¨æˆ·è¿›è¡Œåœ°ç‚¹æ¨èå’Œæ—…è¡Œè§„åˆ’ã€‚ä½ çš„å›ç­”åº”è¯¥ï¼š
1. å‡†ç¡®ã€å®ç”¨ã€æœ‰å¸®åŠ©
2. åŒ…å«å…·ä½“çš„åœ°ç‚¹ä¿¡æ¯ï¼ˆå¦‚æœé€‚ç”¨ï¼‰
3. æä¾›å®ç”¨çš„æ—…è¡Œå»ºè®®
4. ä¿æŒå‹å¥½å’Œä¸“ä¸šçš„è¯­è°ƒ
5. å¦‚æœç”¨æˆ·è¯¢é—®åœ°ç‚¹ï¼Œå°½é‡æä¾›åæ ‡ä¿¡æ¯

å½“æ¨èåœ°ç‚¹æ—¶ï¼Œè¯·æŒ‰ä»¥ä¸‹æ ¼å¼å›å¤ï¼š
åœ°ç‚¹åç§°ï¼š[åç§°]
åœ°å€ï¼š[è¯¦ç»†åœ°å€]
åæ ‡ï¼š[çº¬åº¦,ç»åº¦]
æ¨èç†ç”±ï¼š[ç®€çŸ­æè¿°]`
      },
      ...history.slice(-8), // ä¿ç•™æœ€è¿‘8æ¡å†å²æ¶ˆæ¯
      {
        role: 'user',
        content: message
      }
    ]
    
    // è°ƒç”¨AI API
    const response = await fetch(`${AI_CONFIG.baseURL}/chat/completions`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${AI_CONFIG.apiKey}`
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: AI_CONFIG.model,
        messages,
        temperature: 0.7,
        max_tokens: 1000
      })
    })
    
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`AI API error: ${response.status}`)
    }
    
    const data = await response.json()
    const aiResponse = data.choices[0].message.content
    
    // è§£æAIå›å¤ä¸­çš„ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯
    const locations = extractLocations(aiResponse)
    
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({
      success: true,
      response: aiResponse,
      locations
    }), {
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
      }
    })
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('AI Chat API Error:', error)
    
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({
      success: false,
      error: 'AIæœåŠ¡æš‚æ—¶ä¸å¯ç”¨ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åå†è¯•'
    }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
      }
    })
  }
}

// ä»AIå›å¤ä¸­æå–ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯
function extractLocations(text: string) {
  const locations = []
  const lines = text.split('\n')
  
  let currentLocation: any = {}
  
  for (const line of lines) {
    if (line.includes('åœ°ç‚¹åç§°ï¼š')) {
      if (currentLocation.name) {
        locations.push(currentLocation)
      }
      currentLocation = {
        name: line.replace('åœ°ç‚¹åç§°ï¼š', '').trim()
      }
    } else if (line.includes('åœ°å€ï¼š')) {
      currentLocation.address = line.replace('åœ°å€ï¼š', '').trim()
    } else if (line.includes('åæ ‡ï¼š')) {
      const coords = line.replace('åæ ‡ï¼š', '').trim()
      const [lat, lng] = coords.split(',').map(s => parseFloat(s.trim()))
      if (!isNaN(lat) && !isNaN(lng)) {
        currentLocation.lat = lat
        currentLocation.lng = lng
      }
    } else if (line.includes('æ¨èç†ç”±ï¼š')) {
      currentLocation.description = line.replace('æ¨èç†ç”±ï¼š', '').trim()
    }
  }
  
  if (currentLocation.name) {
    locations.push(currentLocation)
  }
  
  return locations
}
```

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/Chat/AIChatBot.vue
<template>

    <!-- èŠå¤©æ ‡é¢˜ -->
    <div class="chat-header p-4 bg-blue-50 border-b">

           :class="['message', message.role === 'user' ? 'user-message' : 'ai-message']">

            {{ formatTime(message.timestamp) }}
          </div>

      </div>
      
      <!-- AIæ€è€ƒä¸­çŠ¶æ€ -->

        <div class="message-content p-3 rounded-lg bg-gray-100">

            <div class="animate-spin rounded-full h-4 w-4 border-b-2 border-blue-500"></div>

        <el-button size="small" @click="sendQuickMessage('æ¨èé™„è¿‘çš„ç¾é£Ÿ')">
          ğŸ½ï¸ æ¨èç¾é£Ÿ
        </el-button>
        <el-button size="small" @click="sendQuickMessage('æ‰¾ä¸ªå®‰é™çš„å’–å•¡å…')">
          â˜• æ‰¾å’–å•¡å…
        </el-button>
        <el-button size="small" @click="sendQuickMessage('è§„åˆ’ä¸€æ—¥æ¸¸è·¯çº¿')">
          ğŸ—ºï¸ è§„åˆ’è·¯çº¿
        </el-button>
        <el-button size="small" @click="sendQuickMessage('é™„è¿‘æœ‰ä»€ä¹ˆæ™¯ç‚¹')">
          ğŸ›ï¸ æ‰¾æ™¯ç‚¹
        </el-button>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, nextTick, onMounted } from 'vue'
import { ElButton, ElInput, ElIcon, ElMessage } from 'element-plus'
import { ChatDotRound } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
import { useChatStore } from '../../stores/chat'
import { useMapStore } from '../../stores/map'

const chatStore = useChatStore()
const mapStore = useMapStore()
const currentMessage = ref('')
const messagesContainer = ref<HTMLElement>()

// å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯
const sendMessage = async () => {
  if (!currentMessage.value.trim()) return
  
  const message = currentMessage.value.trim()
  currentMessage.value = ''
  
  try {
    await chatStore.sendMessage(message, {
      currentLocation: mapStore.currentLocation,
      locations: mapStore.locations,
      mapCenter: mapStore.mapCenter
    })
    
    // æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°åº•éƒ¨
    await nextTick()
    scrollToBottom()
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·é‡è¯•')
  }
}

// å‘é€å¿«æ·æ¶ˆæ¯
const sendQuickMessage = (message: string) => {
  currentMessage.value = message
  sendMessage()
}

// æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ¶ˆæ¯å†…å®¹
const formatMessage = (content: string) => {
  return content
    .replace(/\n/g, '<br>')
    .replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
    .replace(/\*(.*?)\*/g, '<em>$1</em>')
}

// æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ—¶é—´
const formatTime = (timestamp: string) => {
  return new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString('zh-CN', {
    hour: '2-digit',
    minute: '2-digit'
  })
}

// æ»šåŠ¨åˆ°åº•éƒ¨
const scrollToBottom = () => {
  if (messagesContainer.value) {
    messagesContainer.value.scrollTop = messagesContainer.value.scrollHeight
  }
}

// ç»„ä»¶æŒ‚è½½æ—¶å‘é€æ¬¢è¿æ¶ˆæ¯
onMounted(() => {
  if (chatStore.messages.length === 0) {
    chatStore.addMessage({
      id: Date.now(),
      role: 'assistant',
      content: 'ğŸ‘‹ ä½ å¥½ï¼æˆ‘æ˜¯AIåœ°å›¾åŠ©æ‰‹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¸®ä½ ï¼š\n\nğŸ” **æ™ºèƒ½æ¨èåœ°ç‚¹** - æ ¹æ®ä½ çš„éœ€æ±‚æ¨èé¤å…ã€æ™¯ç‚¹ã€å’–å•¡å…ç­‰\nğŸ—ºï¸ **è§„åˆ’æœ€ä½³è·¯çº¿** - ä¸ºä½ è§„åˆ’é«˜æ•ˆçš„å‡ºè¡Œè·¯çº¿\nğŸ“ **è§£ç­”ä½ç½®é—®é¢˜** - å›ç­”å…³äºåœ°ç‚¹ã€äº¤é€šã€å‘¨è¾¹è®¾æ–½çš„é—®é¢˜\n\nè¯·å‘Šè¯‰æˆ‘ä½ æƒ³å»å“ªé‡Œæˆ–æƒ³åšä»€ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    })
  }
})
</script>
```

#### 2. èŠå¤©çŠ¶æ€ç®¡ç†

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/stores/chat.ts
import { defineStore } from 'pinia'
import { ref } from 'vue'

export interface ChatMessage {
  id: number
  role: 'user' | 'assistant'
  content: string
  timestamp: string
}

export interface ChatContext {
  currentLocation?: { lat: number; lng: number }
  locations?: any[]
  mapCenter?: { lat: number; lng: number }
}

export const useChatStore = defineStore('chat', () => {
  const messages = ref<ChatMessage[]>([])
  const isLoading = ref(false)
  const apiEndpoint = ref('http://localhost:11434/v1/chat/completions')
  
  // æ·»åŠ æ¶ˆæ¯
  const addMessage = (message: ChatMessage) => {
    messages.value.push(message)
  }
  
  // å‘é€æ¶ˆæ¯
  const sendMessage = async (content: string, context?: ChatContext) => {
    // æ·»åŠ ç”¨æˆ·æ¶ˆæ¯
    const userMessage: ChatMessage = {
      id: Date.now(),
      role: 'user',
      content,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }
    addMessage(userMessage)
    
    isLoading.value = true
    
    try {
      // æ„å»ºä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ä¿¡æ¯
      const contextInfo = buildContextInfo(context)
      const systemPrompt = `ä½ æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªä¸“ä¸šçš„åœ°å›¾AIåŠ©æ‰‹ï¼Œä¸“é—¨å¸®åŠ©ç”¨æˆ·å‘ç°æœ‰è¶£çš„åœ°ç‚¹å’Œè§„åˆ’è·¯çº¿ã€‚

å½“å‰ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ï¼š
${contextInfo}

è¯·ç”¨å‹å¥½ã€ä¸“ä¸šçš„è¯­æ°”å›ç­”ç”¨æˆ·é—®é¢˜ã€‚å¦‚æœç”¨æˆ·è¯¢é—®åœ°ç‚¹æ¨èï¼Œè¯·æä¾›å…·ä½“çš„å»ºè®®ã€‚å¦‚æœæ¶‰åŠè·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’ï¼Œè¯·ç»™å‡ºå®ç”¨çš„å»ºè®®ã€‚`

      // è°ƒç”¨AI API
      const response = await fetch(apiEndpoint.value, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          model: 'deepseek-r1:7b',
          messages: [
            { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
            { role: 'user', content }
          ],
          temperature: 0.7,
          max_tokens: 500
        })
      })
      
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`APIè¯·æ±‚å¤±è´¥: ${response.status}`)
      }
      
      const data = await response.json()
      const aiResponse = data.choices[0]?.message?.content || 'æŠ±æ­‰ï¼Œæˆ‘ç°åœ¨æ— æ³•å›ç­”è¿™ä¸ªé—®é¢˜ã€‚'
      
      // æ·»åŠ AIå›å¤
      const aiMessage: ChatMessage = {
        id: Date.now() + 1,
        role: 'assistant',
        content: aiResponse,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      }
      addMessage(aiMessage)
      
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('AI APIè°ƒç”¨å¤±è´¥:', error)
      
      // æ·»åŠ é”™è¯¯å›å¤
      const errorMessage: ChatMessage = {
        id: Date.now() + 1,
        role: 'assistant',
        content: 'æŠ±æ­‰ï¼Œæˆ‘ç°åœ¨é‡åˆ°äº†ä¸€äº›æŠ€æœ¯é—®é¢˜ã€‚è¯·ç¨åå†è¯•ï¼Œæˆ–è€…å°è¯•é‡æ–°æè¿°ä½ çš„é—®é¢˜ã€‚',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      }
      addMessage(errorMessage)
      
      throw error
    } finally {
      isLoading.value = false
    }
  }
  
  // æ„å»ºä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ä¿¡æ¯
  const buildContextInfo = (context?: ChatContext): string => {
    if (!context) return 'æš‚æ— ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯'
    
    let info = ''
    
    if (context.currentLocation) {
      info += `ç”¨æˆ·å½“å‰ä½ç½®: ${context.currentLocation.lat.toFixed(4)}, ${context.currentLocation.lng.toFixed(4)}\n`
    }
    
    if (context.mapCenter) {
      info += `åœ°å›¾ä¸­å¿ƒ: ${context.mapCenter.lat.toFixed(4)}, ${context.mapCenter.lng.toFixed(4)}\n`
    }
    
    if (context.locations && context.locations.length > 0) {
      info += `å·²ä¿å­˜çš„åœ°ç‚¹æ•°é‡: ${context.locations.length}\n`
      info += `æœ€è¿‘çš„åœ°ç‚¹: ${context.locations.slice(-3).map(loc => loc.name).join(', ')}\n`
    }
    
    return info || 'æš‚æ— ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯'
  }
  
  // æ¸…ç©ºèŠå¤©è®°å½•
  const clearMessages = () => {
    messages.value = []
  }
  
  // è®¾ç½®APIç«¯ç‚¹
  const setApiEndpoint = (endpoint: string) => {
    apiEndpoint.value = endpoint
  }
  
  return {
    messages,
    isLoading,
    apiEndpoint,
    addMessage,
    sendMessage,
    clearMessages,
    setApiEndpoint
  }
})
```

```astro:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/pages/index.astro
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </main>
</Layout>
```

```astro:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/pages/index.astro
        const dataApp = createApp(DataManager);
        dataApp.use(pinia);
        dataApp.use(ElementPlus);
        dataApp.mount('#data-manager');
      } catch (error) {
        console.warn('DataManagerç»„ä»¶æœªæ‰¾åˆ°ï¼Œè·³è¿‡æŒ‚è½½');
      }

      try {
```

```bash:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/backup_script.sh
#!/bin/bash

# MAPSXPLRé¡¹ç›®è‡ªåŠ¨å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬
PROJECT_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1"
BACKUP_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/backups"
TIMESTAMP=$(date '+%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')

# åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½ç›®å½•
mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR"

echo "ğŸ”„ å¼€å§‹å¤‡ä»½ MAPSXPLR é¡¹ç›®..."

# 1. Gitå¤‡ä»½
cd "$PROJECT_DIR"
git add .
git commit -m "è‡ªåŠ¨å¤‡ä»½: $TIMESTAMP"
git push origin main

# 2. æ ¸å¿ƒæ–‡ä»¶å¤‡ä»½
tar -czf "$BACKUP_DIR/mapsxplr_core_$TIMESTAMP.tar.gz" \
    --exclude=node_modules \
    --exclude=dist \
    --exclude=.astro \
    --exclude=.git \
    .

# 3. é…ç½®æ–‡ä»¶å•ç‹¬å¤‡ä»½
cp package.json "$BACKUP_DIR/package_$TIMESTAMP.json"
cp astro.config.mjs "$BACKUP_DIR/astro.config_$TIMESTAMP.mjs"
cp -r src/ "$BACKUP_DIR/src_$TIMESTAMP/"

echo "âœ… å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆï¼å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶ä½äº: $BACKUP_DIR"
```

## ğŸ“¦ å¤‡ä»½ç­–ç•¥è¯¦è§£

### 1. Gitç‰ˆæœ¬æ§åˆ¶å¤‡ä»½ï¼ˆä¸»ç­–ç•¥ï¼‰

```bash
# æ¯æ—¥æäº¤è„šæœ¬
#!/bin/bash
# daily_backup.sh

cd /Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1

# æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦æœ‰å˜æ›´

    echo "æ£€æµ‹åˆ°æ–‡ä»¶å˜æ›´ï¼Œå¼€å§‹å¤‡ä»½..."
```

### 2. æ–‡ä»¶ç³»ç»Ÿå¤‡ä»½ï¼ˆè¾…åŠ©ç­–ç•¥ï¼‰

#### å®æ–½æ­¥éª¤

**2.1 åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½ç›®å½•ç»“æ„**

```bash
mkdir -p ~/Backups/MAPSXPLR/{daily,weekly,monthly}
```

**2.2 è‡ªåŠ¨å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬**

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# filesystem_backup.sh

SOURCE_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1"
BACKUP_BASE="$HOME/Backups/MAPSXPLR"
TIMESTAMP=$(date "+%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")

# æ¯æ—¥å¤‡ä»½
daily_backup() {
    BACKUP_DIR="$BACKUP_BASE/daily/mapsxplr_$TIMESTAMP"
    echo "å¼€å§‹æ¯æ—¥å¤‡ä»½åˆ°: $BACKUP_DIR"
    
    rsync -av --exclude='node_modules' \
              --exclude='.git' \
              --exclude='dist' \
              --exclude='.astro' \
              "$SOURCE_DIR/" "$BACKUP_DIR/"
    
    echo "æ¯æ—¥å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆ"
}

# æ¯å‘¨å¤‡ä»½ï¼ˆåŒ…å«ä¾èµ–ï¼‰
weekly_backup() {
    BACKUP_DIR="$BACKUP_BASE/weekly/mapsxplr_week_$TIMESTAMP"
    echo "å¼€å§‹æ¯å‘¨å¤‡ä»½åˆ°: $BACKUP_DIR"
    
    rsync -av --exclude='.git' \
              --exclude='dist' \
              --exclude='.astro' \
              "$SOURCE_DIR/" "$BACKUP_DIR/"
    
    echo "æ¯å‘¨å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆ"
}

# æ ¹æ®å‚æ•°æ‰§è¡Œä¸åŒå¤‡ä»½
case "$1" in
    "daily")
        daily_backup
        ;;
    "weekly")
        weekly_backup
        ;;
    *)
        echo "ç”¨æ³•: $0 {daily|weekly}"
        exit 1
        ;;
esac
```

**2.3 å®šæ—¶ä»»åŠ¡è®¾ç½®**

```bash
# ç¼–è¾‘crontab
crontab -e

# æ·»åŠ ä»¥ä¸‹å†…å®¹
# æ¯å¤©æ™šä¸Š11ç‚¹æ‰§è¡Œæ¯æ—¥å¤‡ä»½
0 23 * * * /path/to/filesystem_backup.sh daily

# æ¯å‘¨æ—¥æ™šä¸Š11:30æ‰§è¡Œæ¯å‘¨å¤‡ä»½
30 23 * * 0 /path/to/filesystem_backup.sh weekly
```

### 3. å¢é‡å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬ï¼ˆå…³é”®èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼‰

#### å®æ–½æ­¥éª¤

**3.1 æ™ºèƒ½å¢é‡å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬**

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# incremental_backup.sh

SOURCE_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1"
BACKUP_BASE="$HOME/Backups/MAPSXPLR/incremental"
TIMESTAMP=$(date "+%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
LAST_BACKUP_FILE="$BACKUP_BASE/.last_backup"

# åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½ç›®å½•
mkdir -p "$BACKUP_BASE"

# æ£€æŸ¥ä¸Šæ¬¡å¤‡ä»½æ—¶é—´
if [[ -f "$LAST_BACKUP_FILE" ]]; then
    LAST_BACKUP=$(cat "$LAST_BACKUP_FILE")
    echo "ä¸Šæ¬¡å¤‡ä»½: $LAST_BACKUP"
else
    echo "é¦–æ¬¡å¢é‡å¤‡ä»½"
    LAST_BACKUP="1970-01-01"
fi

# æŸ¥æ‰¾å˜æ›´æ–‡ä»¶
echo "æŸ¥æ‰¾è‡ª $LAST_BACKUP ä»¥æ¥çš„å˜æ›´æ–‡ä»¶..."
find "$SOURCE_DIR" -type f -newer "$LAST_BACKUP_FILE" 2>/dev/null > /tmp/changed_files.txt

# å¦‚æœæœ‰å˜æ›´ï¼Œæ‰§è¡Œå¤‡ä»½
if [[ -s /tmp/changed_files.txt ]]; then
    BACKUP_DIR="$BACKUP_BASE/inc_$TIMESTAMP"
    mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR"
    
    echo "å‘ç° $(wc -l < /tmp/changed_files.txt) ä¸ªå˜æ›´æ–‡ä»¶"
    
    # å¤åˆ¶å˜æ›´æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œä¿æŒç›®å½•ç»“æ„
    while IFS= read -r file; do
        if [[ -f "$file" ]]; then
            rel_path=${file#$SOURCE_DIR/}
            target_dir="$BACKUP_DIR/$(dirname "$rel_path")"
            mkdir -p "$target_dir"
            cp "$file" "$target_dir/"
        fi
    done < /tmp/changed_files.txt
    
    # åˆ›å»ºå˜æ›´æ¸…å•
    cp /tmp/changed_files.txt "$BACKUP_DIR/changed_files.log"
    
    # æ›´æ–°æœ€åå¤‡ä»½æ—¶é—´
    echo "$TIMESTAMP" > "$LAST_BACKUP_FILE"
    touch "$LAST_BACKUP_FILE"
    
    echo "å¢é‡å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆ: $BACKUP_DIR"
else
    echo "æ— å˜æ›´æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œè·³è¿‡å¤‡ä»½"
fi

# æ¸…ç†ä¸´æ—¶æ–‡ä»¶
rm -f /tmp/changed_files.txt
```

## ğŸ”„ è¿˜åŸèŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸æ“ä½œæŒ‡å—

### 1. å®Œæ•´é¡¹ç›®è¿˜åŸ

#### Gitè¿˜åŸ

```bash
# è¿˜åŸåˆ°ç‰¹å®šæäº¤
git reset --hard <commit-hash>

# è¿˜åŸåˆ°ç‰¹å®šæ ‡ç­¾
git checkout v0.0.1-stable

# å¼ºåˆ¶è¿˜åŸï¼ˆä¸¢å¼ƒæ‰€æœ‰æœ¬åœ°å˜æ›´ï¼‰
git reset --hard origin/main
```

#### æ–‡ä»¶ç³»ç»Ÿè¿˜åŸ

```bash
# ä»æ¯æ—¥å¤‡ä»½è¿˜åŸ
rsync -av ~/Backups/MAPSXPLR/daily/mapsxplr_20250120_230000/ \
          /Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/

# ä»æ¯å‘¨å¤‡ä»½è¿˜åŸ
rsync -av ~/Backups/MAPSXPLR/weekly/mapsxplr_week_20250120_230000/ \
          /Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/
```

### 2. æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½è¿˜åŸ

#### ç»„ä»¶çº§è¿˜åŸè„šæœ¬

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# restore_components.sh

BACKUP_SOURCE="$1"
COMPONENT="$2"
TARGET_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1"

case "$COMPONENT" in
    "map")
        echo "è¿˜åŸåœ°å›¾ç»„ä»¶..."
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/components/MapExplorer.vue" "$TARGET_DIR/src/components/"
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/stores/mapStore.ts" "$TARGET_DIR/src/stores/"
        ;;
    "ai")
        echo "è¿˜åŸAIèŠå¤©ç»„ä»¶..."
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/components/AIChatBot.vue" "$TARGET_DIR/src/components/"
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/stores/chatStore.ts" "$TARGET_DIR/src/stores/"
        ;;
    "route")
        echo "è¿˜åŸè·¯çº¿ç®¡ç†ç»„ä»¶..."
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/components/RouteManager.vue" "$TARGET_DIR/src/components/"
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/stores/routeStore.ts" "$TARGET_DIR/src/stores/"
        ;;
    "data")
        echo "è¿˜åŸæ•°æ®ç®¡ç†ç»„ä»¶..."
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/components/DataManager.vue" "$TARGET_DIR/src/components/"
        cp "$BACKUP_SOURCE/src/stores/dataStore.ts" "$TARGET_DIR/src/stores/"
        ;;
    *)
        echo "ç”¨æ³•: $0 <backup_source> {map|ai|route|data}"
        exit 1
        ;;
esac

echo "ç»„ä»¶è¿˜åŸå®Œæˆ"
```

### 2. å¤‡ä»½å®Œæ•´æ€§éªŒè¯

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# verify_backup.sh

SOURCE_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1"
BACKUP_DIR="$1"

if [[ -z "$BACKUP_DIR" || ! -d "$BACKUP_DIR" ]]; then
    echo "ç”¨æ³•: $0 <backup_directory>"
    exit 1
fi

echo "éªŒè¯å¤‡ä»½å®Œæ•´æ€§: $BACKUP_DIR"
echo

# æ£€æŸ¥å…³é”®æ–‡ä»¶
KEY_FILES=(
    "package.json"
    "astro.config.mjs"
    "src/pages/index.astro"
    "src/components/MapExplorer.vue"
    "src/components/AIChatBot.vue"
    "src/components/RouteManager.vue"
    "src/components/DataManager.vue"
    "src/components/LocationList.vue"
)

MISSING_FILES=()
for file in "${KEY_FILES[@]}"; do
    if [[ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/$file" ]]; then
        echo "âœ… $file"
    else
        echo "âŒ $file (ç¼ºå¤±)"
        MISSING_FILES+=("$file")
    fi
done

echo
if [[ ${#MISSING_FILES[@]} -eq 0 ]]; then
    echo "ğŸ‰ å¤‡ä»½éªŒè¯é€šè¿‡ï¼æ‰€æœ‰å…³é”®æ–‡ä»¶å®Œæ•´ã€‚"
else
    echo "âš ï¸  å‘ç° ${#MISSING_FILES[@]} ä¸ªç¼ºå¤±æ–‡ä»¶:"
    printf '   - %s\n' "${MISSING_FILES[@]}"
fi
```

  ```typescript
}
```

### ğŸ¯ ç«‹å³æ‰§è¡Œä»»åŠ¡

#### 1. ç´§æ€¥ä¿®å¤ï¼šAI APIé›†æˆ

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/pages/api/ai-chat.ts
export async function POST({ request }: { request: Request }) {
  try {
    const { message, context } = await request.json();
    
    // DeepSeek-R1:7b APIé›†æˆ
    const response = await fetch('https://api.deepseek.com/v1/chat/completions', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${import.meta.env.DEEPSEEK_API_KEY}`
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: 'deepseek-r1:7b',
        messages: [
          {
            role: 'system',
            content: 'ä½ æ˜¯MAPSXPLRçš„AIåŠ©æ‰‹ï¼Œä¸“é—¨å¸®åŠ©ç”¨æˆ·è¿›è¡Œåœ°å›¾æ¢ç´¢ã€ä½ç½®ç®¡ç†å’Œè·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’ã€‚è¯·ç”¨ç®€æ´ã€å‹å¥½çš„è¯­è¨€å›ç­”ç”¨æˆ·é—®é¢˜ã€‚'
          },
          {
            role: 'user', 
            content: `${context ? `ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡ä¿¡æ¯ï¼š${JSON.stringify(context)}\n\n` : ''}ç”¨æˆ·é—®é¢˜ï¼š${message}`
          }
        ],
        max_tokens: 1000,
        temperature: 0.7
      })
    });
    
    if (!response.ok) {
      throw new Error(`APIè¯·æ±‚å¤±è´¥: ${response.status}`);
    }
    
    const data = await response.json();
    
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({
      success: true,
      message: data.choices[0].message.content,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }), {
      status: 200,
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
      }
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('AI Chat API Error:', error);
    
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({
      success: false,
      error: 'æŠ±æ­‰ï¼ŒAIæœåŠ¡æš‚æ—¶ä¸å¯ç”¨ï¼Œè¯·ç¨åå†è¯•ã€‚',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
      }
    });
  }
}
```

#### 2. ç¯å¢ƒé…ç½®æ–‡ä»¶

```env:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/.env.example
# AIæœåŠ¡é…ç½®
```

#### 3. åˆ›å»ºç¼ºå¤±çš„å·¥å…·å‡½æ•°

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/utils/geo.ts
import * as turf from '@turf/turf';

// åœ°ç†å·¥å…·å‡½æ•°
export const geoUtils = {
  // è®¡ç®—ä¸¤ç‚¹é—´è·ç¦»
  calculateDistance(lat1: number, lng1: number, lat2: number, lng2: number): number {
    const from = turf.point([lng1, lat1]);
    const to = turf.point([lng2, lat2]);
    return turf.distance(from, to, { units: 'kilometers' });
  },
  
  // æ ¼å¼åŒ–åæ ‡
  formatCoordinates(lat: number, lng: number): string {
    return `${lat.toFixed(6)}, ${lng.toFixed(6)}`;
  },
  
  // éªŒè¯åæ ‡æœ‰æ•ˆæ€§
  isValidCoordinate(lat: number, lng: number): boolean {
    return lat >= -90 && lat <= 90 && lng >= -180 && lng <= 180;
  },
  
  // è®¡ç®—è·¯çº¿æ€»è·ç¦»
  calculateRouteDistance(coordinates: [number, number][]): number {
    if (coordinates.length < 2) return 0;
    
    let totalDistance = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < coordinates.length - 1; i++) {
      const [lng1, lat1] = coordinates[i];
      const [lng2, lat2] = coordinates[i + 1];
      totalDistance += this.calculateDistance(lat1, lng1, lat2, lng2);
    }
    
    return totalDistance;
  }
};
```

```typescript:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/types/index.ts
// ä½ç½®ç›¸å…³ç±»å‹

export interface Route {

  name: string;
  description?: string;
  coordinates: [number, number][];
  distance: number;
  estimatedTime?: number;
  difficulty?: 'easy' | 'medium' | 'hard';
  createdAt: Date;
}

// èŠå¤©æ¶ˆæ¯ç±»å‹
export interface ChatMessage {

  content: string;
  role: 'user' | 'assistant';
  timestamp: Date;
  context?: any;
}

// APIå“åº”ç±»å‹

  data?: T;
  error?: string;
  message?: string;
  timestamp: string;
}

// åœ°å›¾è§†å›¾ç±»å‹

// æ•°æ®å¯¼å‡ºæ ¼å¼
```

### ğŸ“ 2. åœ°å›¾åŠŸèƒ½å¢å¼º

#### ä¼˜åŒ–MapExplorerç»„ä»¶

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/Map/MapExplorer.vue
<template>
  <div class="map-explorer">
    <!-- åœ°å›¾æ§åˆ¶é¢æ¿ -->
    <div class="map-controls mb-4">
      <el-row :gutter="12">
        <el-col :span="6">
          <el-button @click="getCurrentLocation" type="primary" size="small">
            <el-icon><Location /></el-icon>
            å®šä½
          </el-button>
        </el-col>
        <el-col :span="6">
          <el-button @click="clearAllMarkers" size="small">
            <el-icon><Delete /></el-icon>
            æ¸…é™¤
          </el-button>
        </el-col>
        <el-col :span="6">
          <el-select v-model="viewMode" @change="changeMapView" size="small">
            <el-option label="æ ‡å‡†" value="normal" />
            <el-option label="å«æ˜Ÿ" value="satellite" />
            <el-option label="åœ°å½¢" value="terrain" />
          </el-select>
        </el-col>
        <el-col :span="6">
          <el-button @click="showAllMarkers" size="small">
            <el-icon><View /></el-icon>
            å…¨è§ˆ
          </el-button>
        </el-col>
      </el-row>
    </div>
    
    <!-- åœ°å›¾å®¹å™¨ -->
    <div id="map" class="map-container" style="height: 400px; border-radius: 8px;"></div>
    
    <!-- ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯é¢æ¿ -->
    <div v-if="selectedLocation" class="location-info mt-4 p-4 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg">
      <h4 class="font-semibold mb-2">{{ selectedLocation.name }}</h4>
      <p class="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-2">{{ selectedLocation.description }}</p>
      <p class="text-xs text-gray-500">
        åæ ‡: {{ formatCoordinates(selectedLocation.latitude, selectedLocation.longitude) }}
      </p>
      <div class="mt-3">
        <el-button @click="editLocation" size="small" type="primary">ç¼–è¾‘</el-button>
        <el-button @click="deleteLocation" size="small" type="danger">åˆ é™¤</el-button>
      </div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- æ·»åŠ ä½ç½®å¯¹è¯æ¡† -->
    <el-dialog v-model="showAddDialog" title="æ·»åŠ æ–°ä½ç½®" width="400px">
      <el-form :model="newLocation" label-width="80px">
        <el-form-item label="åç§°">
          <el-input v-model="newLocation.name" placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥ä½ç½®åç§°" />
        </el-form-item>
        <el-form-item label="æè¿°">
          <el-input v-model="newLocation.description" type="textarea" placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥ä½ç½®æè¿°" />
        </el-form-item>
        <el-form-item label="åˆ†ç±»">
          <el-select v-model="newLocation.category" placeholder="é€‰æ‹©åˆ†ç±»">
            <el-option label="é¤å…" value="restaurant" />
            <el-option label="æ™¯ç‚¹" value="attraction" />
            <el-option label="ä½å®¿" value="hotel" />
            <el-option label="è´­ç‰©" value="shopping" />
            <el-option label="å…¶ä»–" value="other" />
          </el-select>
        </el-form-item>
        <el-form-item label="æ ‡ç­¾">
          <el-input v-model="newLocation.tags" placeholder="ç”¨é€—å·åˆ†éš”å¤šä¸ªæ ‡ç­¾" />
        </el-form-item>
      </el-form>
      <template #footer>
        <el-button @click="showAddDialog = false">å–æ¶ˆ</el-button>
        <el-button @click="saveNewLocation" type="primary">ä¿å­˜</el-button>
      </template>
    </el-dialog>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, onMounted, nextTick } from 'vue';
import { useMapStore } from '../../stores/map';
import { geoUtils } from '../../utils/geo';
import L from 'leaflet';
import { ElMessage } from 'element-plus';
import { Location, Delete, View } from '@element-plus/icons-vue';

const mapStore = useMapStore();
const map = ref<L.Map | null>(null);
const viewMode = ref('normal');
const selectedLocation = ref(null);
const showAddDialog = ref(false);
const newLocation = ref({
  name: '',
  description: '',
  category: '',
  tags: '',
  latitude: 0,
  longitude: 0
});

// åœ°å›¾å›¾å±‚é…ç½®
const mapLayers = {
  normal: L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png'),
  satellite: L.tileLayer('https://server.arcgisonline.com/ArcGIS/rest/services/World_Imagery/MapServer/tile/{z}/{y}/{x}'),
  terrain: L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.opentopomap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png')
};

onMounted(() => {
  initMap();
});

function initMap() {
  nextTick(() => {
    // åˆå§‹åŒ–åœ°å›¾
    map.value = L.map('map').setView([39.9042, 116.4074], 13);
    
    // æ·»åŠ é»˜è®¤å›¾å±‚
    mapLayers.normal.addTo(map.value);
    
    // åœ°å›¾ç‚¹å‡»äº‹ä»¶
    map.value.on('click', (e: L.LeafletMouseEvent) => {
      const { lat, lng } = e.latlng;
      newLocation.value.latitude = lat;
      newLocation.value.longitude = lng;
      showAddDialog.value = true;
    });
    
    // åŠ è½½å·²ä¿å­˜çš„ä½ç½®
    loadSavedLocations();
    
    mapStore.setMapInstance(map.value);
  });
}

function getCurrentLocation() {
  if (navigator.geolocation) {
    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
      (position) => {
        const { latitude, longitude } = position.coords;
        map.value?.setView([latitude, longitude], 15);
        
        // æ·»åŠ å½“å‰ä½ç½®æ ‡è®°
        const marker = L.marker([latitude, longitude])
          .addTo(map.value!)
          .bindPopup('æ‚¨çš„å½“å‰ä½ç½®')
          .openPopup();
          
        mapStore.setCurrentLocation({ latitude, longitude });
        ElMessage.success('å®šä½æˆåŠŸ');
      },
      (error) => {
        ElMessage.error('å®šä½å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·æ£€æŸ¥ä½ç½®æƒé™');
      }
    );
  } else {
    ElMessage.error('æµè§ˆå™¨ä¸æ”¯æŒåœ°ç†å®šä½');
  }
}

function changeMapView(mode: string) {
  if (map.value) {
    // ç§»é™¤å½“å‰å›¾å±‚
    map.value.eachLayer((layer) => {
      if (layer instanceof L.TileLayer) {
        map.value!.removeLayer(layer);
      }
    });
    
    // æ·»åŠ æ–°å›¾å±‚
    mapLayers[mode as keyof typeof mapLayers].addTo(map.value);
  }
}

function clearAllMarkers() {
  if (map.value) {
    map.value.eachLayer((layer) => {
      if (layer instanceof L.Marker) {
        map.value!.removeLayer(layer);
      }
    });
    mapStore.clearAllLocations();
    ElMessage.success('å·²æ¸…é™¤æ‰€æœ‰æ ‡è®°');
  }
}

function showAllMarkers() {
  const locations = mapStore.locations;
  if (locations.length > 0) {
    const group = new L.FeatureGroup(locations.map(loc => 
      L.marker([loc.latitude, loc.longitude])
    ));
    map.value?.fitBounds(group.getBounds().pad(0.1));
  }
}

function loadSavedLocations() {
  mapStore.locations.forEach(location => {
    addMarkerToMap(location);
  });
}

function addMarkerToMap(location: any) {
  if (map.value) {
    const marker = L.marker([location.latitude, location.longitude])
      .addTo(map.value)
      .bindPopup(`
        <div>
          <h4>${location.name}</h4>
          <p>${location.description || ''}</p>
          <small>${formatCoordinates(location.latitude, location.longitude)}</small>
        </div>
      `);
      
    marker.on('click', () => {
      selectedLocation.value = location;
    });
  }
}

function saveNewLocation() {
  if (!newLocation.value.name.trim()) {
    ElMessage.error('è¯·è¾“å…¥ä½ç½®åç§°');
    return;
  }
  
  const location = {
    id: Date.now().toString(),
    name: newLocation.value.name,
    description: newLocation.value.description,
    category: newLocation.value.category,
    tags: newLocation.value.tags.split(',').map(tag => tag.trim()).filter(Boolean),
    latitude: newLocation.value.latitude,
    longitude: newLocation.value.longitude,
    createdAt: new Date(),
    updatedAt: new Date()
  };
  
  mapStore.addLocation(location);
  addMarkerToMap(location);
  
  // é‡ç½®è¡¨å•
  newLocation.value = {
    name: '',
    description: '',
    category: '',
    tags: '',
    latitude: 0,
    longitude: 0
  };
  
  showAddDialog.value = false;
  ElMessage.success('ä½ç½®å·²ä¿å­˜');
}

function editLocation() {
  // ç¼–è¾‘ä½ç½®é€»è¾‘
  ElMessage.info('ç¼–è¾‘åŠŸèƒ½å¼€å‘ä¸­');
}

function deleteLocation() {
  if (selectedLocation.value) {
    mapStore.removeLocation(selectedLocation.value.id);
    // ä»åœ°å›¾ç§»é™¤æ ‡è®°
    map.value?.eachLayer((layer) => {
      if (layer instanceof L.Marker) {
        const pos = layer.getLatLng();
        if (pos.lat === selectedLocation.value.latitude && 
            pos.lng === selectedLocation.value.longitude) {
          map.value!.removeLayer(layer);
        }
      }
    });
    selectedLocation.value = null;
    ElMessage.success('ä½ç½®å·²åˆ é™¤');
  }
}

function formatCoordinates(lat: number, lng: number): string {
  return geoUtils.formatCoordinates(lat, lng);
}
</script>

<style scoped>
.map-explorer {
  width: 100%;
}

.map-container {
  border: 1px solid #e5e7eb;
}

.location-info {
  border: 1px solid #e5e7eb;
}
</style>
```

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/Data/DataManager.vue
            <div v-if="selectedFile" class="mt-2">

                ç¡®è®¤å¯¼å…¥

      <!-- äº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥ -->
      <el-card header="äº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥" class="mt-4">
        <div class="sync-status mb-3">
          <el-tag :type="syncStatus === 'synced' ? 'success' : 'warning'">
            {{ syncStatusText }}
          </el-tag>

        <el-row :gutter="12">
          <el-col :span="8">
            <el-button @click="syncToCloud" :loading="syncing" type="primary" size="small" block>
              ä¸Šä¼ åˆ°äº‘ç«¯

              {{ autoSync ? 'å…³é—­' : 'å¼€å¯' }}è‡ªåŠ¨åŒæ­¥
            </el-button>

      </el-card>
      
      <!-- æ•°æ®å¤‡ä»½ -->
      <el-card header="æ•°æ®å¤‡ä»½" class="mt-4">

              åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½

              ç®¡ç†å¤‡ä»½
            </el-button>

      </el-card>

    <!-- å¤‡ä»½åˆ—è¡¨å¯¹è¯æ¡† -->
    <el-dialog v-model="showBackups" title="å¤‡ä»½ç®¡ç†" width="500px">

        <div v-for="backup in backups" :key="backup.id" class="backup-item">
          <div class="backup-info">
            <h4>{{ backup.name }}</h4>

          </div>

              æ¢å¤

              åˆ é™¤

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed, onMounted } from 'vue';
import { useDataStore } from '../../stores/data';
import { useMapStore } from '../../stores/map';
import { useRouteStore } from '../../stores/route';
import { ElMessage, ElMessageBox } from 'element-plus';
import { Download, Upload, FolderAdd, Folder } from '@element-plus/icons-vue';
import { geoUtils } from '../../utils/geo';

const dataStore = useDataStore();
const mapStore = useMapStore();
const routeStore = useRouteStore();

const exportFormat = ref('json');
const selectedFile = ref(null);
const uploadRef = ref();
const syncing = ref(false);
const syncStatus = ref('pending');
const autoSync = ref(false);
const showBackups = ref(false);
const backups = ref([]);

const totalDistance = computed(() => {
  return routeStore.routes.reduce((total, route) => total + route.distance, 0);
});

const storageUsed = computed(() => {
  const data = JSON.stringify({
    locations: mapStore.locations,
    routes: routeStore.routes
  });
  return (new Blob([data]).size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2);
});

const syncStatusText = computed(() => {
  switch (syncStatus.value) {
    case 'synced': return 'å·²åŒæ­¥';
    case 'pending': return 'å¾…åŒæ­¥';
    case 'error': return 'åŒæ­¥å¤±è´¥';
    default: return 'æœªçŸ¥çŠ¶æ€';
  }
});

const lastSyncTime = computed(() => {
  return dataStore.lastSyncTime ? 
    new Date(dataStore.lastSyncTime).toLocaleString() : null;
});

onMounted(() => {
  loadBackups();
});

function exportData() {
  const data = {
    locations: mapStore.locations,
    routes: routeStore.routes,
    exportTime: new Date().toISOString(),
    version: '1.0.0'
  };
  
  let content: string;
  let filename: string;
  let mimeType: string;
  
  switch (exportFormat.value) {
    case 'json':
      content = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2);
      filename = `mapsxplr-data-${Date.now()}.json`;
      mimeType = 'application/json';
      break;
      
    case 'gpx':
      content = dataStore.exportToGPX(data.locations);
      filename = `mapsxplr-locations-${Date.now()}.gpx`;
      mimeType = 'application/gpx+xml';
      break;
      
    case 'kml':
      content = dataStore.exportToKML(data.locations);
      filename = `mapsxplr-locations-${Date.now()}.kml`;
      mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-earth.kml+xml';
      break;
      
    case 'csv':
      content = exportToCSV(data.locations);
      filename = `mapsxplr-locations-${Date.now()}.csv`;
      mimeType = 'text/csv';
      break;
      
    default:
      ElMessage.error('ä¸æ”¯æŒçš„å¯¼å‡ºæ ¼å¼');
      return;
  }
  
  downloadFile(content, filename, mimeType);
  ElMessage.success('æ•°æ®å¯¼å‡ºæˆåŠŸ');
}

function exportToCSV(locations: any[]): string {
  const headers = ['åç§°', 'æè¿°', 'çº¬åº¦', 'ç»åº¦', 'åˆ†ç±»', 'æ ‡ç­¾', 'åˆ›å»ºæ—¶é—´'];
  const rows = locations.map(loc => [
    loc.name,
    loc.description || '',
    loc.latitude,
    loc.longitude,
    loc.category || '',
    (loc.tags || []).join(';'),
    new Date(loc.createdAt).toLocaleString()
  ]);
  
  return [headers, ...rows]
    .map(row => row.map(cell => `"${cell}"`).join(','))
    .join('\n');
}

function downloadFile(content: string, filename: string, mimeType: string) {
  const blob = new Blob([content], { type: mimeType });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = url;
  link.download = filename;
  document.body.appendChild(link);
  link.click();
  document.body.removeChild(link);
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

function handleFileChange(file: any) {
  selectedFile.value = file;
}

async function importData() {
  if (!selectedFile.value) {
    ElMessage.error('è¯·å…ˆé€‰æ‹©æ–‡ä»¶');
    return;
  }
  
  try {
    const content = await readFileContent(selectedFile.value.raw);
    const extension = selectedFile.value.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase();
    
    let importedData;
    
    switch (extension) {
      case 'json':
        importedData = JSON.parse(content);
        break;
        
      case 'gpx':
        importedData = await dataStore.parseGPX(content);
        break;
        
      case 'kml':
        importedData = await dataStore.parseKML(content);
        break;
        
      case 'csv':
        importedData = parseCSV(content);
        break;
        
      default:
        throw new Error('ä¸æ”¯æŒçš„æ–‡ä»¶æ ¼å¼');
    }
    
    // ç¡®è®¤å¯¼å…¥
    await ElMessageBox.confirm(
      `ç¡®å®šè¦å¯¼å…¥ ${importedData.locations?.length || 0} ä¸ªä½ç½®å—ï¼Ÿ`,
      'ç¡®è®¤å¯¼å…¥',
      { type: 'warning' }
    );
    
    // æ‰§è¡Œå¯¼å…¥
    if (importedData.locations) {
      importedData.locations.forEach((location: any) => {
        mapStore.addLocation({
          ...location,
          id: Date.now().toString() + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)
        });
      });
    }
    
    if (importedData.routes) {
      importedData.routes.forEach((route: any) => {
        routeStore.addRoute({
          ...route,
          id: Date.now().toString() + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)
        });
      });
    }
    
    selectedFile.value = null;
    ElMessage.success('æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥æˆåŠŸ');
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('å¯¼å…¥å¤±è´¥:', error);
    ElMessage.error('å¯¼å…¥å¤±è´¥: ' + error.message);
  }
}

function readFileContent(file: File): Promise<string> {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (e) => resolve(e.target?.result as string);
    reader.onerror = reject;
    reader.readAsText(file);
  });
}

function parseCSV(content: string): any {
  const lines = content.split('\n');
  const headers = lines[0].split(',').map(h => h.replace(/"/g, ''));
  
  const locations = lines.slice(1)
    .filter(line => line.trim())
    .map(line => {
      const values = line.split(',').map(v => v.replace(/"/g, ''));
      return {
        name: values[0],
        description: values[1],
        latitude: parseFloat(values[2]),
        longitude: parseFloat(values[3]),
        category: values[4],
        tags: values[5] ? values[5].split(';') : [],
        createdAt: new Date(values[6] || Date.now()),
        updatedAt: new Date()
      };
    });
    
  return { locations };
}

async function syncToCloud() {
  syncing.value = true;
  try {
    // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿäº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
    
    dataStore.updateSyncTime();
    syncStatus.value = 'synced';
    ElMessage.success('æ•°æ®å·²åŒæ­¥åˆ°äº‘ç«¯');
  } catch (error) {
    syncStatus.value = 'error';
    ElMessage.error('åŒæ­¥å¤±è´¥');
  } finally {
    syncing.value = false;
  }
}

async function syncFromCloud() {
  syncing.value = true;
  try {
    // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿä»äº‘ç«¯ä¸‹è½½
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
    
    ElMessage.success('æ•°æ®å·²ä»äº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥');
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('åŒæ­¥å¤±è´¥');
  } finally {
    syncing.value = false;
  }
}

function toggleAutoSync() {
  autoSync.value = !autoSync.value;
  ElMessage.success(`è‡ªåŠ¨åŒæ­¥å·²${autoSync.value ? 'å¼€å¯' : 'å…³é—­'}`);
}

function createBackup() {
  const backup = {
    id: Date.now().toString(),
    name: `å¤‡ä»½-${new Date().toLocaleString()}`,
    data: {
      locations: mapStore.locations,
      routes: routeStore.routes
    },
    createdAt: new Date(),
    size: storageUsed.value + 'MB'
  };
  
  backups.value.unshift(backup);
  localStorage.setItem('mapsxplr-backups', JSON.stringify(backups.value));
  ElMessage.success('å¤‡ä»½åˆ›å»ºæˆåŠŸ');
}

function showBackupList() {
  showBackups.value = true;
}

function loadBackups() {
  const saved = localStorage.getItem('mapsxplr-backups');
  if (saved) {
    backups.value = JSON.parse(saved);
  }
}

async function restoreBackup(backup: any) {
  try {
    await ElMessageBox.confirm(
      'æ¢å¤å¤‡ä»½å°†è¦†ç›–å½“å‰æ‰€æœ‰æ•°æ®ï¼Œç¡®å®šç»§ç»­å—ï¼Ÿ',
      'ç¡®è®¤æ¢å¤',
      { type: 'warning' }
    );
    
    // æ¸…é™¤å½“å‰æ•°æ®
    mapStore.clearAllLocations();
    routeStore.clearAllRoutes();
    
    // æ¢å¤å¤‡ä»½æ•°æ®
    backup.data.locations.forEach((location: any) => {
      mapStore.addLocation(location);
    });
    
    backup.data.routes.forEach((route: any) => {
      routeStore.addRoute(route);
    });
    
    showBackups.value = false;
    ElMessage.success('å¤‡ä»½æ¢å¤æˆåŠŸ');
    
  } catch (error) {
    // ç”¨æˆ·å–æ¶ˆ
  }
}

function deleteBackup(backupId: string) {
  backups.value = backups.value.filter(b => b.id !== backupId);
  localStorage.setItem('mapsxplr-backups', JSON.stringify(backups.value));
  ElMessage.success('å¤‡ä»½å·²åˆ é™¤');
}

function formatDate(date: Date): string {
  return new Date(date).toLocaleString();
}
</script>

<style scoped>
.stats-grid {
  display: grid;
  grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(120px, 1fr));
  gap: 1rem;
}

.stat-card {
  background: white;

}

}
</style>
```

### ğŸ›£ï¸ 4. è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’åŸå‹å¼€å‘

#### åˆ›å»ºRouteManagerç»„ä»¶

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/Route/RouteManager.vue
<template>
  <div class="route-manager">
    <!-- è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’æ§åˆ¶é¢æ¿ -->
    <div class="route-controls mb-4">
      <el-button @click="startPlanning" type="primary" size="small" :disabled="planning">
        <el-icon><Guide /></el-icon>
        {{ planning ? 'è§„åˆ’ä¸­...' : 'å¼€å§‹è§„åˆ’' }}
      </el-button>
      <el-button @click="optimizeRoute" size="small" :disabled="!currentRoute || optimizing">
        <el-icon><Refresh /></el-icon>
        {{ optimizing ? 'ä¼˜åŒ–ä¸­...' : 'ä¼˜åŒ–è·¯çº¿' }}
      </el-button>
      <el-button @click="clearRoute" size="small" :disabled="!currentRoute">
        <el-icon><Delete /></el-icon>
        æ¸…é™¤è·¯çº¿
      </el-button>
    </div>
    
    <!-- è·¯çº¿ä¿¡æ¯ -->
    <div v-if="currentRoute" class="route-info mb-4 p-3 bg-blue-50 rounded-lg">
      <h4 class="font-semibold mb-2">å½“å‰è·¯çº¿</h4>
      <div class="route-stats">
        <div class="stat-item">

          ä¿å­˜è·¯çº¿

          åˆ†äº«è·¯çº¿
        </el-button>

    </div>
    
    <!-- è·¯çº¿åˆ—è¡¨ -->
    <div class="saved-routes">
      <h4 class="font-semibold mb-3">å·²ä¿å­˜è·¯çº¿</h4>
      <div v-if="routeStore.routes.length === 0" class="empty-state text-center py-4 text-gray-500">
        <el-icon size="48"><MapLocation /></el-icon>

              åŠ è½½

              ç¼–è¾‘
            </el-button>

              åˆ é™¤
            </el-button>
          </div>
        </div>
```
