```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1/src/components/Route/RouteManager.vue
    </div>
    
    <!-- ä¿å­˜è·¯çº¿å¯¹è¯æ¡† -->
    <el-dialog v-model="showSaveDialog" title="ä¿å­˜è·¯çº¿" width="400px">
      <el-form :model="routeForm" label-width="80px">
        <el-form-item label="è·¯çº¿åç§°">
          <el-input v-model="routeForm.name" placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥è·¯çº¿åç§°" />
        </el-form-item>

          <el-input v-model="routeForm.description" type="textarea" placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥è·¯çº¿æè¿°" />

        <el-form-item label="éš¾åº¦">
          <el-select v-model="routeForm.difficulty" placeholder="é€‰æ‹©éš¾åº¦">
            <el-option label="ç®€å•" value="easy" />
            <el-option label="ä¸­ç­‰" value="medium" />
            <el-option label="å›°éš¾" value="hard" />

      <template #footer>
        <el-button @click="showSaveDialog = false">å–æ¶ˆ</el-button>
        <el-button @click="confirmSaveRoute" type="primary">ä¿å­˜</el-button>
      </template>
    </el-dialog>
  </div>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed } from 'vue';
import { useRouteStore } from '../../stores/route';
import { useMapStore } from '../../stores/map';
import { ElMessage, ElMessageBox } from 'element-plus';
import { Guide, Refresh, Delete, Check, Share, MapLocation } from '@element-plus/icons-vue';
import { geoUtils } from '../../utils/geo';

const routeStore = useRouteStore();
const mapStore = useMapStore();

const planning = ref(false);
const optimizing = ref(false);
const showSaveDialog = ref(false);
const routeForm = ref({
  name: '',
  description: '',
  difficulty: 'medium'
});

const currentRoute = computed(() => routeStore.currentRoute);

const estimatedTime = computed(() => {
  if (!currentRoute.value) return '0åˆ†é’Ÿ';
  
  // å‡è®¾å¹³å‡é€Ÿåº¦ä¸º5km/hï¼ˆæ­¥è¡Œï¼‰
  const hours = currentRoute.value.distance / 5;
  const minutes = Math.round(hours * 60);
  
  if (minutes < 60) {
    return `${minutes}åˆ†é’Ÿ`;
  } else {
    const h = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
    const m = minutes % 60;
    return `${h}å°æ—¶${m}åˆ†é’Ÿ`;
  }
});

async function startPlanning() {
  const locations = mapStore.locations;
  
  if (locations.length < 2) {
    ElMessage.warning('è‡³å°‘éœ€è¦2ä¸ªä½ç½®æ‰èƒ½è§„åˆ’è·¯çº¿');
    return;
  }
  
  planning.value = true;
  
  try {
    // ä½¿ç”¨æœ€è¿‘é‚»ç®—æ³•è¿›è¡Œç®€å•è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’
    const coordinates = locations.map(loc => [loc.longitude, loc.latitude]);
    const distance = geoUtils.calculateRouteDistance(coordinates);
    
    const route = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      name: `è·¯çº¿-${new Date().toLocaleString()}`,
      coordinates,
      distance,
      createdAt: new Date()
    };
    
    routeStore.setCurrentRoute(route);
    ElMessage.success('è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’å®Œæˆ');
    
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’å¤±è´¥');
  } finally {
    planning.value = false;
  }
}

async function optimizeRoute() {
  if (!currentRoute.value) return;
  
  optimizing.value = true;
  
  try {
    // æ¨¡æ‹ŸTSPä¼˜åŒ–ç®—æ³•
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1500));
    
    // ç®€å•çš„2-optä¼˜åŒ–ï¼ˆè¿™é‡Œåªæ˜¯æ¨¡æ‹Ÿï¼‰
    const optimizedRoute = {
      ...currentRoute.value,
      distance: currentRoute.value.distance * 0.9, // å‡è®¾ä¼˜åŒ–åè·ç¦»å‡å°‘10%
    };
    
    routeStore.setCurrentRoute(optimizedRoute);
    ElMessage.success('è·¯çº¿ä¼˜åŒ–å®Œæˆï¼Œè·ç¦»å‡å°‘äº†10%');
    
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('è·¯çº¿ä¼˜åŒ–å¤±è´¥');
  } finally {
    optimizing.value = false;
  }
}

function clearRoute() {
  routeStore.clearCurrentRoute();
  ElMessage.success('è·¯çº¿å·²æ¸…é™¤');
}

function saveRoute() {
  if (!currentRoute.value) return;
  
  routeForm.value = {
    name: currentRoute.value.name || `è·¯çº¿-${new Date().toLocaleString()}`,
    description: '',
    difficulty: 'medium'
  };
  
  showSaveDialog.value = true;
}

function confirmSaveRoute() {
  if (!routeForm.value.name.trim()) {
    ElMessage.error('è¯·è¾“å…¥è·¯çº¿åç§°');
    return;
  }
  
  const route = {
    ...currentRoute.value,
    name: routeForm.value.name,
    description: routeForm.value.description,
    difficulty: routeForm.value.difficulty,
    id: Date.now().toString()
  };
  
  routeStore.addRoute(route);
  showSaveDialog.value = false;
  ElMessage.success('è·¯çº¿å·²ä¿å­˜');
}

function shareRoute() {
  if (!currentRoute.value) return;
  
  // ç”Ÿæˆåˆ†äº«é“¾æ¥ï¼ˆæ¨¡æ‹Ÿï¼‰
  const shareData = {
    name: currentRoute.value.name,
    coordinates: currentRoute.value.coordinates,
    distance: currentRoute.value.distance
  };
  
  const shareUrl = `${window.location.origin}/route/shared?data=${encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(shareData))}`;
  
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(shareUrl).then(() => {
    ElMessage.success('åˆ†äº«é“¾æ¥å·²å¤åˆ¶åˆ°å‰ªè´´æ¿');
  }).catch(() => {
    ElMessage.error('å¤åˆ¶å¤±è´¥ï¼Œè¯·æ‰‹åŠ¨å¤åˆ¶é“¾æ¥');
  });
}

function loadRoute(route: any) {
  routeStore.setCurrentRoute(route);
  ElMessage.success(`å·²åŠ è½½è·¯çº¿: ${route.name}`);
}

function editRoute(route: any) {
  ElMessage.info('ç¼–è¾‘åŠŸèƒ½å¼€å‘ä¸­');
}

async function deleteRoute(routeId: string) {
  try {
    await ElMessageBox.confirm(
      'ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤è¿™æ¡è·¯çº¿å—ï¼Ÿ',
      'ç¡®è®¤åˆ é™¤',
      { type: 'warning' }
    );
    
    routeStore.removeRoute(routeId);
    ElMessage.success('è·¯çº¿å·²åˆ é™¤');
    
  } catch (error) {
    // ç”¨æˆ·å–æ¶ˆ
  }
}

function getDifficultyText(difficulty: string): string {
  switch (difficulty) {
    case 'easy': return 'ç®€å•';
    case 'medium': return 'ä¸­ç­‰';
    case 'hard': return 'å›°éš¾';
    default: return 'æœªçŸ¥';
  }
}
</script>

<style scoped>

}
```

### ğŸ”„ 6. è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬

#### åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬

```bash:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/backup.sh
#!/bin/bash

# MAPSXPLRé¡¹ç›®è‡ªåŠ¨å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬
# ä½¿ç”¨æ–¹æ³•: ./backup.sh [backup-type]

set -e

PROJECT_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_202507201916-v0.0.1"
BACKUP_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/backups"
TIMESTAMP=$(date +%Y%m%d%H%M)
BACKUP_TYPE=${1:-"full"}

echo "ğŸ”’ å¼€å§‹æ‰§è¡ŒMAPSXPLRé¡¹ç›®å¤‡ä»½..."
echo "å¤‡ä»½ç±»å‹: $BACKUP_TYPE"
echo "æ—¶é—´æˆ³: $TIMESTAMP"

# åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½ç›®å½•
mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR/{files,git,docs,config}/$TIMESTAMP"

cd "$PROJECT_DIR"

# 1. æ–‡ä»¶å¤‡ä»½
if [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "full" ] || [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "files" ]; then
    echo "ğŸ“ æ‰§è¡Œæ–‡ä»¶å¤‡ä»½..."
    tar -czf "$BACKUP_DIR/files/$TIMESTAMP/project-$TIMESTAMP.tar.gz" \
        --exclude='node_modules' \
        --exclude='.git' \
        --exclude='dist' \
        --exclude='.astro' \
        .
    echo "âœ… æ–‡ä»¶å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆ"
fi

# 2. Gitå¤‡ä»½
if [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "full" ] || [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "git" ]; then
    echo "ğŸ”§ æ‰§è¡ŒGitå¤‡ä»½..."
    
    # æäº¤å½“å‰æ›´æ”¹
    git add .
    git commit -m "backup: è‡ªåŠ¨å¤‡ä»½ $TIMESTAMP" || true
    
    # åˆ›å»ºå¤‡ä»½åˆ†æ”¯
    git checkout -b "backup/auto-$TIMESTAMP" || true
    git push origin "backup/auto-$TIMESTAMP" || true
    git checkout main
    
    # å¯¼å‡ºGitå†å²
    git log --oneline > "$BACKUP_DIR/git/$TIMESTAMP/git-history.txt"
    git branch -a > "$BACKUP_DIR/git/$TIMESTAMP/branches.txt"
    git tag > "$BACKUP_DIR/git/$TIMESTAMP/tags.txt"
    
    echo "âœ… Gitå¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆ"
fi

# 3. é…ç½®å¤‡ä»½
if [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "full" ] || [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "config" ]; then
    echo "âš™ï¸ æ‰§è¡Œé…ç½®å¤‡ä»½..."
    
    cp package.json "$BACKUP_DIR/config/$TIMESTAMP/"
    cp tsconfig.json "$BACKUP_DIR/config/$TIMESTAMP/"
    cp astro.config.mjs "$BACKUP_DIR/config/$TIMESTAMP/"
    cp .env.example "$BACKUP_DIR/config/$TIMESTAMP/"
    
    # ç”Ÿæˆä¾èµ–æ¸…å•
    npm list --depth=0 > "$BACKUP_DIR/config/$TIMESTAMP/dependencies.txt" 2>/dev/null || true
    
    echo "âœ… é…ç½®å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆ"
fi

# 4. æ–‡æ¡£å¤‡ä»½
if [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "full" ] || [ "$BACKUP_TYPE" = "docs" ]; then
    echo "ğŸ“š æ‰§è¡Œæ–‡æ¡£å¤‡ä»½..."
    
    cp README.md "$BACKUP_DIR/docs/$TIMESTAMP/"
    cp -r docs/ "$BACKUP_DIR/docs/$TIMESTAMP/" 2>/dev/null || true
    
    # ç”Ÿæˆé¡¹ç›®ç»“æ„
    tree -I 'node_modules|.git|dist|.astro' > "$BACKUP_DIR/docs/$TIMESTAMP/structure.txt" 2>/dev/null || \
    find . -type f -not -path './node_modules/*' -not -path './.git/*' > "$BACKUP_DIR/docs/$TIMESTAMP/files.txt"
    
    echo "âœ… æ–‡æ¡£å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆ"
fi

# 5. æ¸…ç†æ—§å¤‡ä»½ï¼ˆä¿ç•™æœ€è¿‘10ä¸ªï¼‰
echo "ğŸ§¹ æ¸…ç†æ—§å¤‡ä»½..."
find "$BACKUP_DIR" -name "*.tar.gz" -mtime +30 -delete 2>/dev/null || true
find "$BACKUP_DIR" -type d -empty -delete 2>/dev/null || true

echo "ğŸ‰ å¤‡ä»½å®Œæˆï¼"
echo "å¤‡ä»½ä½ç½®: $BACKUP_DIR"
echo "å¤‡ä»½å¤§å°: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR | cut -f1)"

# ç”Ÿæˆå¤‡ä»½æŠ¥å‘Š
cat > "$BACKUP_DIR/backup-report-$TIMESTAMP.txt" << EOF
MAPSXPLRé¡¹ç›®å¤‡ä»½æŠ¥å‘Š
==================

å¤‡ä»½æ—¶é—´: $(date)
å¤‡ä»½ç±»å‹: $BACKUP_TYPE
é¡¹ç›®ç‰ˆæœ¬: v0.0.2-beta-preview

å¤‡ä»½å†…å®¹:
- é¡¹ç›®æ–‡ä»¶: $([ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/files/$TIMESTAMP/project-$TIMESTAMP.tar.gz" ] && echo "âœ…" || echo "âŒ")
- Gitå†å²: $([ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/git/$TIMESTAMP/git-history.txt" ] && echo "âœ…" || echo "âŒ")
- é…ç½®æ–‡ä»¶: $([ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/config/$TIMESTAMP/package.json" ] && echo "âœ…" || echo "âŒ")
- æ–‡æ¡£èµ„æ–™: $([ -f "$BACKUP_DIR/docs/$TIMESTAMP/README.md" ] && echo "âœ…" || echo "âŒ")

å¤‡ä»½ä½ç½®: $BACKUP_DIR
æ€»å¤§å°: $(du -sh $BACKUP_DIR | cut -f1)

EOF

echo "ğŸ“‹ å¤‡ä»½æŠ¥å‘Šå·²ç”Ÿæˆ: $BACKUP_DIR/backup-report-$TIMESTAMP.txt"
```

### ğŸ“Š 8. å¤‡ä»½éªŒè¯

#### éªŒè¯è„šæœ¬

```bash:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/verify-backup.sh
#!/bin/bash

# å¤‡ä»½éªŒè¯è„šæœ¬

BACKUP_DIR="/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/backups"
LATEST_BACKUP=$(ls -t "$BACKUP_DIR"/files/*/project-*.tar.gz 2>/dev/null | head -1)

if [ -z "$LATEST_BACKUP" ]; then
    echo "âŒ æœªæ‰¾åˆ°å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶"
    exit 1
fi

echo "ğŸ” éªŒè¯æœ€æ–°å¤‡ä»½: $LATEST_BACKUP"

# æ£€æŸ¥å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶å®Œæ•´æ€§
if tar -tzf "$LATEST_BACKUP" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo "âœ… å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶å®Œæ•´æ€§éªŒè¯é€šè¿‡"
else
    echo "âŒ å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶æŸå"
    exit 1
fi

# æ£€æŸ¥å…³é”®æ–‡ä»¶
KEY_FILES=("package.json" "src/pages/index.astro" "src/components/Map/MapExplorer.vue")

for file in "${KEY_FILES[@]}"; do
    if tar -tzf "$LATEST_BACKUP" | grep -q "$file"; then
        echo "âœ… å…³é”®æ–‡ä»¶å­˜åœ¨: $file"
    else
        echo "âŒ å…³é”®æ–‡ä»¶ç¼ºå¤±: $file"
    fi
done

echo "ğŸ‰ å¤‡ä»½éªŒè¯å®Œæˆ"
```

```bash
   ./backup.sh full
   ```

## æ¦‚è¿°

æœ¬æ–‡æ¡£æä¾›äº†MAPSXPLRé¡¹ç›®çš„å®Œæ•´å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼Œç¡®ä¿å¼€å‘è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­çš„é‡è¦å¯¹è¯è®°å½•å¾—åˆ°å¦¥å–„ä¿å­˜å’Œç®¡ç†ã€‚

- **é¡¹ç›®ç®¡ç†**: è¿›åº¦è·Ÿè¸ªã€ä»»åŠ¡åˆ†é…ã€é‡Œç¨‹ç¢‘è§„åˆ’
- **é—®é¢˜è§£å†³**: Bugä¿®å¤ã€æ€§èƒ½ä¼˜åŒ–ã€æ•…éšœæ’æŸ¥
- **çŸ¥è¯†åˆ†äº«**: æŠ€æœ¯æ–‡æ¡£ã€æœ€ä½³å®è·µã€ç»éªŒæ€»ç»“

### 2. å¤‡ä»½é¢‘ç‡

- **å®æ—¶å¤‡ä»½**: é‡è¦æŠ€æœ¯å†³ç­–å’Œå…³é”®å¯¹è¯

## è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–è„šæœ¬

### 1. å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬ (backup-chat.sh)

```bash:chat-backups/scripts/backup-chat.sh
#!/bin/bash

# å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½è„šæœ¬
set -e

# é…ç½®
BACKUP_DIR="/path/to/chat-backups"
TEMPLATE_DIR="$BACKUP_DIR/templates"
DATE=$(date +"%Y%m%d")
TIMESTAMP=$(date +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

# åˆ›å»ºç›®å½•ç»“æ„
create_directory_structure() {
    local year=$(date +"%Y")
    local month=$(date +"%m-%B")
    
    mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR/$year/$month/development"
    mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR/$year/$month/project-management"
    mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR/$year/$month/debugging"
    mkdir -p "$BACKUP_DIR/$year/$month/knowledge-sharing"
}

# åˆ›å»ºæ–°çš„å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶
create_chat_backup() {
    local chat_type=$1
    local topic=$2
    local filename="CHAT_MAPSXPLR_${chat_type^^}_${DATE}_v1.0.md"
    local year=$(date +"%Y")
    local month=$(date +"%m-%B")
    local type_dir=""
    
    case $chat_type in
        "dev") type_dir="development" ;;
        "pm") type_dir="project-management" ;;
        "debug") type_dir="debugging" ;;
        "ks") type_dir="knowledge-sharing" ;;
        *) echo "æœªçŸ¥çš„å¯¹è¯ç±»å‹: $chat_type"; exit 1 ;;
    esac
    
    local filepath="$BACKUP_DIR/$year/$month/$type_dir/$filename"
    
    # å¤åˆ¶æ¨¡æ¿å¹¶æ›¿æ¢å ä½ç¬¦
    cp "$TEMPLATE_DIR/chat-backup-template.md" "$filepath"
    sed -i "s/\[å¯¹è¯ä¸»é¢˜\]/$topic/g" "$filepath"
    sed -i "s/YYYY-MM-DD/$(date +"%Y-%m-%d")/g" "$filepath"
    
    echo "å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶å·²åˆ›å»º: $filepath"
    echo "è¯·ç¼–è¾‘æ–‡ä»¶å¹¶æ·»åŠ å¯¹è¯å†…å®¹"
}

# æ›´æ–°ç´¢å¼•
update_index() {
    local filepath=$1
    local chat_type=$2
    local topic=$3
    
    # æ›´æ–°JSONç´¢å¼•
    python3 "$BACKUP_DIR/scripts/organize-chats.py" --update-index "$filepath" "$chat_type" "$topic"
}

# ä¸»å‡½æ•°
main() {
    if [ $# -lt 2 ]; then
        echo "ç”¨æ³•: $0 <å¯¹è¯ç±»å‹> <å¯¹è¯ä¸»é¢˜>"
        echo "å¯¹è¯ç±»å‹: dev, pm, debug, ks"
        echo "ç¤ºä¾‹: $0 dev 'åœ°å›¾ç»„ä»¶ä¼˜åŒ–è®¨è®º'"
        exit 1
    fi
    
    local chat_type=$1
    local topic=$2
    
    create_directory_structure
    create_chat_backup "$chat_type" "$topic"
    
    echo "å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½åˆ›å»ºå®Œæˆ!"
}

main "$@"
```

### 2. å¯¹è¯ç»„ç»‡è„šæœ¬ (organize-chats.py)

```python:chat-backups/scripts/organize-chats.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import os
import json
import argparse
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path

class ChatOrganizer:
    def __init__(self, backup_dir):
        self.backup_dir = Path(backup_dir)
        self.index_file = self.backup_dir / "index" / "chat-index.json"
        self.tag_index_file = self.backup_dir / "index" / "tag-index.json"
        
    def scan_chat_files(self):
        """æ‰«ææ‰€æœ‰å¯¹è¯æ–‡ä»¶"""
        chat_files = []
        for root, dirs, files in os.walk(self.backup_dir):
            for file in files:
                if file.startswith("CHAT_") and file.endswith(".md"):
                    filepath = Path(root) / file
                    chat_files.append(filepath)
        return chat_files
    
    def parse_chat_metadata(self, filepath):
        """è§£æå¯¹è¯æ–‡ä»¶çš„å…ƒæ•°æ®"""
        with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        metadata = {
            'filepath': str(filepath),
            'filename': filepath.name,
            'size': filepath.stat().st_size,
            'created': datetime.fromtimestamp(filepath.stat().st_ctime).isoformat(),
            'modified': datetime.fromtimestamp(filepath.stat().st_mtime).isoformat()
        }
        
        # è§£ææ–‡ä»¶å†…å®¹ä¸­çš„å…ƒæ•°æ®
        lines = content.split('\n')
        for line in lines:
            if line.startswith('- **é¡¹ç›®**:'):
                metadata['project'] = line.split(':')[1].strip()
            elif line.startswith('- **å¯¹è¯ç±»å‹**:'):
                metadata['chat_type'] = line.split(':')[1].strip()
            elif line.startswith('- **æ—¥æœŸ**:'):
                metadata['date'] = line.split(':')[1].strip()
            elif line.startswith('- **å‚ä¸è€…**:'):
                metadata['participants'] = line.split(':')[1].strip()
            elif line.startswith('- **æ ‡ç­¾**:'):
                tags = line.split(':')[1].strip()
                metadata['tags'] = [tag.strip() for tag in tags.split(',') if tag.strip()]
        
        return metadata
    
    def update_index(self):
        """æ›´æ–°ç´¢å¼•æ–‡ä»¶"""
        chat_files = self.scan_chat_files()
        index_data = []
        tag_index = {}
        
        for filepath in chat_files:
            try:
                metadata = self.parse_chat_metadata(filepath)
                index_data.append(metadata)
                
                # æ›´æ–°æ ‡ç­¾ç´¢å¼•
                tags = metadata.get('tags', [])
                for tag in tags:
                    if tag not in tag_index:
                        tag_index[tag] = []
                    tag_index[tag].append(str(filepath))
                    
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"è§£ææ–‡ä»¶å¤±è´¥ {filepath}: {e}")
        
        # ä¿å­˜ç´¢å¼•
        os.makedirs(self.index_file.parent, exist_ok=True)
        
        with open(self.index_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(index_data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        
        with open(self.tag_index_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(tag_index, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        
        print(f"ç´¢å¼•å·²æ›´æ–°: {len(index_data)} ä¸ªå¯¹è¯æ–‡ä»¶")
        print(f"æ ‡ç­¾ç´¢å¼•: {len(tag_index)} ä¸ªæ ‡ç­¾")
    
    def search_chats(self, query, chat_type=None, date_range=None):
        """æœç´¢å¯¹è¯"""
        with open(self.index_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            index_data = json.load(f)
        
        results = []
        for chat in index_data:
            # ç±»å‹è¿‡æ»¤
            if chat_type and chat.get('chat_type') != chat_type:
                continue
            
            # æ—¥æœŸèŒƒå›´è¿‡æ»¤
            if date_range:
                # å®ç°æ—¥æœŸèŒƒå›´è¿‡æ»¤é€»è¾‘
                pass
            
            # å…³é”®è¯æœç´¢
            if query.lower() in chat.get('filename', '').lower():
                results.append(chat)
                continue
            
            # åœ¨æ ‡ç­¾ä¸­æœç´¢
            tags = chat.get('tags', [])
            if any(query.lower() in tag.lower() for tag in tags):
                results.append(chat)
        
        return results

def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='å¯¹è¯æ–‡ä»¶ç»„ç»‡å·¥å…·')
    parser.add_argument('--backup-dir', default='/path/to/chat-backups', help='å¤‡ä»½ç›®å½•è·¯å¾„')
    parser.add_argument('--update-index', action='store_true', help='æ›´æ–°ç´¢å¼•')
    parser.add_argument('--search', help='æœç´¢å…³é”®è¯')
    parser.add_argument('--type', help='å¯¹è¯ç±»å‹è¿‡æ»¤')
    
    args = parser.parse_args()
    
    organizer = ChatOrganizer(args.backup_dir)
    
    if args.update_index:
        organizer.update_index()
    
    if args.search:
        results = organizer.search_chats(args.search, args.type)
        print(f"æ‰¾åˆ° {len(results)} ä¸ªåŒ¹é…çš„å¯¹è¯:")
        for result in results:
            print(f"- {result['filename']} ({result['date']})")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

### 3. å¯¹è¯æœç´¢è„šæœ¬ (search-chats.py)

```python:chat-backups/scripts/search-chats.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import os
import json
import argparse
from pathlib import Path
import re

class ChatSearcher:
    def __init__(self, backup_dir):
        self.backup_dir = Path(backup_dir)
        self.index_file = self.backup_dir / "index" / "chat-index.json"
    
    def full_text_search(self, query, case_sensitive=False):
        """å…¨æ–‡æœç´¢"""
        results = []
        flags = 0 if case_sensitive else re.IGNORECASE
        pattern = re.compile(query, flags)
        
        for root, dirs, files in os.walk(self.backup_dir):
            for file in files:
                if file.startswith("CHAT_") and file.endswith(".md"):
                    filepath = Path(root) / file
                    try:
                        with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                            content = f.read()
                        
                        matches = pattern.findall(content)
                        if matches:
                            # è·å–åŒ¹é…çš„ä¸Šä¸‹æ–‡
                            lines = content.split('\n')
                            match_lines = []
                            for i, line in enumerate(lines):
                                if pattern.search(line):
                                    start = max(0, i-2)
                                    end = min(len(lines), i+3)
                                    context = '\n'.join(lines[start:end])
                                    match_lines.append({
                                        'line_number': i+1,
                                        'context': context
                                    })
                            
                            results.append({
                                'filepath': str(filepath),
                                'filename': file,
                                'matches': len(matches),
                                'match_lines': match_lines
                            })
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"æœç´¢æ–‡ä»¶å¤±è´¥ {filepath}: {e}")
        
        return results
    
    def search_by_metadata(self, **criteria):
        """æ ¹æ®å…ƒæ•°æ®æœç´¢"""
        try:
            with open(self.index_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                index_data = json.load(f)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("ç´¢å¼•æ–‡ä»¶ä¸å­˜åœ¨ï¼Œè¯·å…ˆè¿è¡Œ organize-chats.py --update-index")
            return []
        
        results = []
        for chat in index_data:
            match = True
            for key, value in criteria.items():
                if key not in chat or chat[key] != value:
                    match = False
                    break
            if match:
                results.append(chat)
        
        return results

def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='å¯¹è¯æœç´¢å·¥å…·')
    parser.add_argument('--backup-dir', default='/path/to/chat-backups', help='å¤‡ä»½ç›®å½•è·¯å¾„')
    parser.add_argument('--query', help='æœç´¢å…³é”®è¯')
    parser.add_argument('--full-text', action='store_true', help='å…¨æ–‡æœç´¢')
    parser.add_argument('--case-sensitive', action='store_true', help='åŒºåˆ†å¤§å°å†™')
    parser.add_argument('--type', help='å¯¹è¯ç±»å‹')
    parser.add_argument('--date', help='æ—¥æœŸ (YYYY-MM-DD)')
    parser.add_argument('--project', help='é¡¹ç›®åç§°')
    
    args = parser.parse_args()
    
    searcher = ChatSearcher(args.backup_dir)
    
    if args.full_text and args.query:
        results = searcher.full_text_search(args.query, args.case_sensitive)
        print(f"å…¨æ–‡æœç´¢ç»“æœ ({len(results)} ä¸ªæ–‡ä»¶):")
        for result in results:
            print(f"\næ–‡ä»¶: {result['filename']}")
            print(f"åŒ¹é…æ¬¡æ•°: {result['matches']}")
            for match in result['match_lines'][:3]:  # åªæ˜¾ç¤ºå‰3ä¸ªåŒ¹é…
                print(f"è¡Œ {match['line_number']}:")
                print(match['context'])
                print("-" * 40)
    
    # å…ƒæ•°æ®æœç´¢
    criteria = {}
    if args.type:
        criteria['chat_type'] = args.type
    if args.date:
        criteria['date'] = args.date
    if args.project:
        criteria['project'] = args.project
    
    if criteria:
        results = searcher.search_by_metadata(**criteria)
        print(f"\nå…ƒæ•°æ®æœç´¢ç»“æœ ({len(results)} ä¸ªæ–‡ä»¶):")
        for result in results:
            print(f"- {result['filename']} ({result.get('date', 'N/A')})")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

- ç¡®ä¿ä¿®å¤ååŠŸèƒ½æ­£å¸¸

### 5. å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½æ–¹æ¡ˆåˆ¶å®šé˜¶æ®µ

**ç”¨æˆ·**: å»ºè®®ï¼ˆå¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½æ–¹æ¡ˆã€‹ï¼›CommonMarkæ–‡æ¡£

**AIåŠ©æ‰‹**: åˆ¶å®šäº†å®Œæ•´çš„å¯¹è¯å¤‡ä»½æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

#### å¤‡ä»½ç­–ç•¥

- å¯¹è¯åˆ†ç±»ï¼ˆå¼€å‘ã€é¡¹ç›®ç®¡ç†ã€é—®é¢˜è§£å†³ã€çŸ¥è¯†åˆ†äº«ï¼‰
- å¤‡ä»½é¢‘ç‡ï¼ˆå®æ—¶ã€æ¯æ—¥ã€æ¯å‘¨ã€é‡Œç¨‹ç¢‘ï¼‰
- æ–‡ä»¶å‘½åè§„èŒƒå’Œç›®å½•ç»“æ„

#### è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–å·¥å…·

- æ–‡æ¡£ç»“æ„æ¨¡æ¿
- å…ƒæ•°æ®æ ‡å‡†
- æœç´¢å’Œåˆ†ç±»ä½“ç³»
- ç»´æŠ¤è®¡åˆ’å’Œæ•…éšœæ¢å¤

# PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR å¯¹è¯å¯¼å‡ºè®°å½•_2025-07-21-v0.0.0

- **æ–‡æ¡£ç±»å‹**: å¯¹è¯å¯¼å‡ºè®°å½•
- **åˆ›å»ºæ—¥æœŸ**: 2025-07-21
- **æ–‡æ¡£ç‰ˆæœ¬**: v0.0.0
- **å¯¼å‡ºèŒƒå›´**: å®Œæ•´å¯¹è¯å†å²
- **æ–‡æ¡£æ ¼å¼**: Markdown (CommonMark)

## å¯¼å‡ºæ‘˜è¦

æœ¬æ–‡æ¡£åŒ…å«MAPSXPLRé¡¹ç›®å¼€å‘è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­çš„å®Œæ•´å¯¹è¯è®°å½•ï¼Œæ¶µç›–ä»é¡¹ç›®åˆå§‹åŒ–åˆ°å½“å‰é˜¶æ®µçš„æ‰€æœ‰é‡è¦æŠ€æœ¯è®¨è®ºã€å†³ç­–è¿‡ç¨‹å’Œé—®é¢˜è§£å†³æ–¹æ¡ˆã€‚

### å¯¹è¯ç»Ÿè®¡

- **æ€»å¯¹è¯è½®æ¬¡**: çº¦50+è½®
- **ä¸»è¦è¯é¢˜**: æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½å¼€å‘ã€å¤‡ä»½æ–¹æ¡ˆã€å®‰å…¨ä¿®å¤ã€å¯¹è¯ç®¡ç†
- **æŠ€æœ¯æ ˆ**: Vue 3, Astro, Leaflet, TypeScript
- **å¼€å‘é˜¶æ®µ**: MVPå¼€å‘é˜¶æ®µ

## å®Œæ•´å¯¹è¯è®°å½•

### ç¬¬ä¸€é˜¶æ®µï¼šé¡¹ç›®åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½å¼€å‘

#### å¯¹è¯1ï¼šé¡¹ç›®å¯åŠ¨

**ç”¨æˆ·**: ç»§ç»­å®Œå–„å‰©ä½™çš„æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½æ¨¡å—ã€‚

**AIåŠ©æ‰‹**: æˆ‘å°†ç»§ç»­å®Œå–„MAPSXPLRé¡¹ç›®çš„æ ¸å¿ƒåŠŸèƒ½æ¨¡å—ã€‚åŸºäºä¹‹å‰çš„å¼€å‘è¿›åº¦ï¼Œæˆ‘éœ€è¦é‡ç‚¹å®Œå–„ä»¥ä¸‹å‡ ä¸ªå…³é”®ç»„ä»¶ï¼š

1. **MapExplorer.vue** - åœ°å›¾äº¤äº’ç»„ä»¶å¢å¼º
2. **DataManager.vue** - æ•°æ®ç®¡ç†ç³»ç»Ÿå®Œå–„
3. **RouteManager.vue** - è·¯çº¿è§„åˆ’åŠŸèƒ½å®ç°

è®©æˆ‘é€ä¸€å®Œå–„è¿™äº›æ ¸å¿ƒæ¨¡å—ï¼š

#### MapExplorer.vue å¢å¼ºåŠŸèƒ½

é¦–å…ˆä¼˜åŒ–åœ°å›¾æ¢ç´¢ç»„ä»¶ï¼Œå¢åŠ æ›´å¤šäº¤äº’åŠŸèƒ½å’Œæ§åˆ¶é€‰é¡¹ï¼š

```vue:/Users/huijoohwee/Documents/GitHub/299_project-test/PRJT0001_MAPSXPLR_MVP_20250120-v0.0.0/src/components/MapExplorer.vue
<template>
  <div class="map-explorer">
    <!-- åœ°å›¾å®¹å™¨ -->
    <div id="map" class="map-container"></div>
    
    <!-- åœ°å›¾æ§åˆ¶é¢æ¿ -->
    <div class="map-controls">
      <div class="control-group">
        <button @click="getCurrentLocation" class="control-btn" title="å®šä½åˆ°å½“å‰ä½ç½®">
          <i class="fas fa-crosshairs"></i>
        </button>
        <button @click="clearAllMarkers" class="control-btn" title="æ¸…é™¤æ‰€æœ‰æ ‡è®°">
          <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
        </button>
        <button @click="toggleMapView" class="control-btn" title="åˆ‡æ¢åœ°å›¾è§†å›¾">
          <i class="fas fa-layer-group"></i>
        </button>
        <button @click="fitAllMarkers" class="control-btn" title="æŸ¥çœ‹å…¨éƒ¨æ ‡è®°">
          <i class="fas fa-expand-arrows-alt"></i>
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯é¢æ¿ -->
    <div v-if="selectedLocation" class="location-info-panel">
      <div class="panel-header">
        <h3>ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯</h3>
        <button @click="closeLocationPanel" class="close-btn">
          <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
        </button>
      </div>
      <div class="panel-content">
        <div class="info-item">
          <label>åç§°:</label>
          <span>{{ selectedLocation.name }}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="info-item">
          <label>åæ ‡:</label>
          <span>{{ selectedLocation.lat.toFixed(6) }}, {{ selectedLocation.lng.toFixed(6) }}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="info-item">
          <label>æè¿°:</label>
          <span>{{ selectedLocation.description || 'æ— æè¿°' }}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="info-item">
          <label>æ·»åŠ æ—¶é—´:</label>
          <span>{{ formatDate(selectedLocation.timestamp) }}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="panel-actions">
          <button @click="editLocation" class="action-btn edit">
            <i class="fas fa-edit"></i> ç¼–è¾‘
          </button>
          <button @click="deleteLocation" class="action-btn delete">
            <i class="fas fa-trash"></i> åˆ é™¤
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- æ·»åŠ æ–°ä½ç½®å¯¹è¯æ¡† -->
    <div v-if="showAddLocationDialog" class="add-location-dialog">
      <div class="dialog-overlay" @click="closeAddLocationDialog"></div>
      <div class="dialog-content">
        <div class="dialog-header">
          <h3>æ·»åŠ æ–°ä½ç½®</h3>
          <button @click="closeAddLocationDialog" class="close-btn">
            <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
          </button>
        </div>
        <div class="dialog-body">
          <div class="form-group">
            <label>ä½ç½®åç§°:</label>
            <input 
              v-model="newLocation.name" 
              type="text" 
              placeholder="è¾“å…¥ä½ç½®åç§°"
              class="form-input"
            >
          </div>
          <div class="form-group">
            <label>æè¿°:</label>
            <textarea 
              v-model="newLocation.description" 
              placeholder="è¾“å…¥ä½ç½®æè¿°ï¼ˆå¯é€‰ï¼‰"
              class="form-textarea"
            ></textarea>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group">
            <label>åæ ‡:</label>
            <div class="coordinate-inputs">
              <input 
                v-model="newLocation.lat" 
                type="number" 
                step="any"
                placeholder="çº¬åº¦"
                class="form-input coordinate"
              >
              <input 
                v-model="newLocation.lng" 
                type="number" 
                step="any"
                placeholder="ç»åº¦"
                class="form-input coordinate"
              >
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="dialog-footer">
          <button @click="closeAddLocationDialog" class="btn-cancel">
            å–æ¶ˆ
          </button>
          <button @click="saveNewLocation" class="btn-save">
            ä¿å­˜ä½ç½®
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, onMounted, onUnmounted, watch } from 'vue'
import L from 'leaflet'
import 'leaflet/dist/leaflet.css'
import { useLocationStore } from '../stores/locationStore'
import { useNotificationStore } from '../stores/notificationStore'

// å­˜å‚¨å¼•ç”¨
const locationStore = useLocationStore()
const notificationStore = useNotificationStore()

// å“åº”å¼æ•°æ®
const map = ref<L.Map | null>(null)
const markers = ref<L.Marker[]>([])
const selectedLocation = ref<any>(null)
const showAddLocationDialog = ref(false)
const currentMapView = ref('street')
const newLocation = ref({
  name: '',
  description: '',
  lat: 0,
  lng: 0
})

// åœ°å›¾å›¾å±‚
const mapLayers = {
  street: L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
    attribution: 'Â© OpenStreetMap contributors'
  }),
  satellite: L.tileLayer('https://server.arcgisonline.com/ArcGIS/rest/services/World_Imagery/MapServer/tile/{z}/{y}/{x}', {
    attribution: 'Â© Esri'
  }),
  terrain: L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.opentopomap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
    attribution: 'Â© OpenTopoMap contributors'
  })
}

// åˆå§‹åŒ–åœ°å›¾
const initMap = () => {
  map.value = L.map('map').setView([39.9042, 116.4074], 10)
  
  // æ·»åŠ é»˜è®¤å›¾å±‚
  mapLayers.street.addTo(map.value)
  
  // åœ°å›¾ç‚¹å‡»äº‹ä»¶
  map.value.on('click', onMapClick)
  
  // åŠ è½½å·²ä¿å­˜çš„ä½ç½®
  loadSavedLocations()
}

// åœ°å›¾ç‚¹å‡»å¤„ç†
const onMapClick = (e: L.LeafletMouseEvent) => {
  newLocation.value.lat = e.latlng.lat
  newLocation.value.lng = e.latlng.lng
  showAddLocationDialog.value = true
}

// è·å–å½“å‰ä½ç½®
const getCurrentLocation = () => {
  if (navigator.geolocation) {
    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
      (position) => {
        const lat = position.coords.latitude
        const lng = position.coords.longitude
        map.value?.setView([lat, lng], 15)
        
        // æ·»åŠ å½“å‰ä½ç½®æ ‡è®°
        const marker = L.marker([lat, lng])
          .addTo(map.value!)
          .bindPopup('æ‚¨çš„å½“å‰ä½ç½®')
          .openPopup()
        
        notificationStore.addNotification({
          type: 'success',
          message: 'å·²å®šä½åˆ°æ‚¨çš„å½“å‰ä½ç½®'
        })
      },
      (error) => {
        notificationStore.addNotification({
          type: 'error',
          message: 'æ— æ³•è·å–å½“å‰ä½ç½®ï¼š' + error.message
        })
      }
    )
  } else {
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'error',
      message: 'æ‚¨çš„æµè§ˆå™¨ä¸æ”¯æŒåœ°ç†å®šä½'
    })
  }
}

// æ¸…é™¤æ‰€æœ‰æ ‡è®°
const clearAllMarkers = () => {
  markers.value.forEach(marker => {
    map.value?.removeLayer(marker)
  })
  markers.value = []
  selectedLocation.value = null
  
  notificationStore.addNotification({
    type: 'info',
    message: 'å·²æ¸…é™¤æ‰€æœ‰åœ°å›¾æ ‡è®°'
  })
}

// åˆ‡æ¢åœ°å›¾è§†å›¾
const toggleMapView = () => {
  const viewTypes = ['street', 'satellite', 'terrain']
  const currentIndex = viewTypes.indexOf(currentMapView.value)
  const nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % viewTypes.length
  const nextView = viewTypes[nextIndex]
  
  // ç§»é™¤å½“å‰å›¾å±‚
  map.value?.removeLayer(mapLayers[currentMapView.value as keyof typeof mapLayers])
  
  // æ·»åŠ æ–°å›¾å±‚
  mapLayers[nextView as keyof typeof mapLayers].addTo(map.value!)
  
  currentMapView.value = nextView
  
  const viewNames = {
    street: 'è¡—é“åœ°å›¾',
    satellite: 'å«æ˜Ÿåœ°å›¾',
    terrain: 'åœ°å½¢åœ°å›¾'
  }
  
  notificationStore.addNotification({
    type: 'info',
    message: `å·²åˆ‡æ¢åˆ°${viewNames[nextView as keyof typeof viewNames]}`
  })
}

// é€‚åº”æ‰€æœ‰æ ‡è®°
const fitAllMarkers = () => {
  if (markers.value.length === 0) {
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'warning',
      message: 'åœ°å›¾ä¸Šæ²¡æœ‰æ ‡è®°ç‚¹'
    })
    return
  }
  
  const group = new L.FeatureGroup(markers.value)
  map.value?.fitBounds(group.getBounds().pad(0.1))
  
  notificationStore.addNotification({
    type: 'info',
    message: `å·²è°ƒæ•´è§†å›¾ä»¥æ˜¾ç¤ºæ‰€æœ‰ ${markers.value.length} ä¸ªæ ‡è®°ç‚¹`
  })
}

// åŠ è½½å·²ä¿å­˜çš„ä½ç½®
const loadSavedLocations = () => {
  const locations = locationStore.getAllLocations()
  
  locations.forEach(location => {
    addMarkerToMap(location)
  })
}

// æ·»åŠ æ ‡è®°åˆ°åœ°å›¾
const addMarkerToMap = (location: any) => {
  const marker = L.marker([location.lat, location.lng])
    .addTo(map.value!)
    .bindPopup(`
      <div class="marker-popup">
        <h4>${location.name}</h4>
        <p>${location.description || 'æ— æè¿°'}</p>
        <small>æ·»åŠ æ—¶é—´: ${formatDate(location.timestamp)}</small>
      </div>
    `)
  
  marker.on('click', () => {
    selectedLocation.value = location
  })
  
  markers.value.push(marker)
}

// ä¿å­˜æ–°ä½ç½®
const saveNewLocation = () => {
  if (!newLocation.value.name.trim()) {
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'error',
      message: 'è¯·è¾“å…¥ä½ç½®åç§°'
    })
    return
  }
  
  const location = {
    id: Date.now().toString(),
    name: newLocation.value.name.trim(),
    description: newLocation.value.description.trim(),
    lat: newLocation.value.lat,
    lng: newLocation.value.lng,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  }
  
  // ä¿å­˜åˆ°å­˜å‚¨
  locationStore.addLocation(location)
  
  // æ·»åŠ åˆ°åœ°å›¾
  addMarkerToMap(location)
  
  // å…³é—­å¯¹è¯æ¡†
  closeAddLocationDialog()
  
  notificationStore.addNotification({
    type: 'success',
    message: `ä½ç½® "${location.name}" å·²ä¿å­˜`
  })
}

// å…³é—­æ·»åŠ ä½ç½®å¯¹è¯æ¡†
const closeAddLocationDialog = () => {
  showAddLocationDialog.value = false
  newLocation.value = {
    name: '',
    description: '',
    lat: 0,
    lng: 0
  }
}

// å…³é—­ä½ç½®ä¿¡æ¯é¢æ¿
const closeLocationPanel = () => {
  selectedLocation.value = null
}

// ç¼–è¾‘ä½ç½®
const editLocation = () => {
  // å®ç°ç¼–è¾‘åŠŸèƒ½
  console.log('ç¼–è¾‘ä½ç½®:', selectedLocation.value)
}

// åˆ é™¤ä½ç½®
const deleteLocation = () => {
  if (selectedLocation.value) {
    locationStore.removeLocation(selectedLocation.value.id)
    
    // ä»åœ°å›¾ç§»é™¤æ ‡è®°
    const markerIndex = markers.value.findIndex(marker => {
      const markerLatLng = marker.getLatLng()
      return markerLatLng.lat === selectedLocation.value.lat && 
             markerLatLng.lng === selectedLocation.value.lng
    })
    
    if (markerIndex !== -1) {
      map.value?.removeLayer(markers.value[markerIndex])
      markers.value.splice(markerIndex, 1)
    }
    
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'success',
      message: `ä½ç½® "${selectedLocation.value.name}" å·²åˆ é™¤`
    })
    
    selectedLocation.value = null
  }
}

// æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ—¥æœŸ
const formatDate = (dateString: string) => {
  return new Date(dateString).toLocaleString('zh-CN')
}

// ç”Ÿå‘½å‘¨æœŸ
onMounted(() => {
  initMap()
})

onUnmounted(() => {
  if (map.value) {
    map.value.remove()
  }
})

// ç›‘å¬ä½ç½®å˜åŒ–
watch(() => locationStore.locations, () => {
  // é‡æ–°åŠ è½½æ ‡è®°
  clearAllMarkers()
  loadSavedLocations()
}, { deep: true })
</script>

<style scoped>
.map-explorer {
  position: relative;
  width: 100%;
  height: 100%;
}

.map-container {
  width: 100%;
  height: 100%;
  border-radius: 8px;
  overflow: hidden;
}

.map-controls {
  position: absolute;
  top: 10px;
  right: 10px;
  z-index: 1000;
}

.control-group {
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  gap: 5px;
}

.control-btn {
  width: 40px;
  height: 40px;
  background: white;
  border: 2px solid #ddd;
```

        </button>

    <!-- æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥ -->
    <div class="import-section">
      <h3>æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥</h3>
      <div class="import-area">
        <div class="file-upload">
          <input 
            ref="fileInput" 
            type="file"

            accept=".json,.gpx,.kml,.csv"
            class="file-input"
          >
          <div class="upload-zone" @click="triggerFileSelect" @dragover.prevent @drop="handleFileDrop">
            <div class="upload-icon">
              <i class="fas fa-cloud-upload-alt"></i>
            </div>
            <div class="upload-text">
              <p>ç‚¹å‡»é€‰æ‹©æ–‡ä»¶æˆ–æ‹–æ‹½æ–‡ä»¶åˆ°æ­¤å¤„</p>

          <small>æœ€ååŒæ­¥: {{ lastSyncTime || 'ä»æœªåŒæ­¥' }}</small>

        <div class="sync-actions">
          <button @click="uploadToCloud" class="sync-btn upload" :disabled="isSyncing">

            <i class="fas fa-sync-alt"></i>

          </button>

    <!-- æ•°æ®å¤‡ä»½ -->

          <div v-if="backups.length === 0" class="no-backups">

            <p>æš‚æ— å¤‡ä»½æ–‡ä»¶</p>

          </button>

<script setup lang="ts">
import { ref, computed, onMounted } from 'vue'
import { useLocationStore } from '../stores/locationStore'
import { useRouteStore } from '../stores/routeStore'
import { useNotificationStore } from '../stores/notificationStore'

// å­˜å‚¨å¼•ç”¨
const locationStore = useLocationStore()
const routeStore = useRouteStore()
const notificationStore = useNotificationStore()

// å“åº”å¼æ•°æ®
const exportFormat = ref('json')
const exportOptions = ref({
  locations: true,
  routes: true,
  settings: false
})
const isExporting = ref(false)
const isImporting = ref(false)
const importFile = ref<File | null>(null)
const fileInput = ref<HTMLInputElement | null>(null)
const syncStatus = ref('disconnected') // connected, syncing, disconnected, error
const isSyncing = ref(false)
const autoSyncEnabled = ref(false)
const lastSyncTime = ref('')
const backups = ref<any[]>([])
const isCreatingBackup = ref(false)

// è®¡ç®—å±æ€§
const locationStats = computed(() => {
  const locations = locationStore.getAllLocations()
  return {
    total: locations.length,
    recent: locations.filter(l => {
      const date = new Date(l.timestamp)
      const weekAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)
      return date > weekAgo
    }).length
  }
})

const routeStats = computed(() => {
  const routes = routeStore.getAllRoutes()
  const totalDistance = routes.reduce((sum, route) => sum + (route.distance || 0), 0)
  return {
    total: routes.length,
    totalDistance: Math.round(totalDistance * 100) / 100
  }
})

const storageStats = computed(() => {
  // ä¼°ç®—æœ¬åœ°å­˜å‚¨ä½¿ç”¨é‡
  const data = {
    locations: locationStore.getAllLocations(),
    routes: routeStore.getAllRoutes()
  }
  const dataString = JSON.stringify(data)
  const sizeInBytes = new Blob([dataString]).size
  const sizeInMB = Math.round(sizeInBytes / 1024 / 1024 * 100) / 100
  
  return {
    used: sizeInMB,
    total: 5 // å‡è®¾æ€»é™åˆ¶ä¸º5MB
  }
})

// æ•°æ®å¯¼å‡º
const exportData = async () => {
  isExporting.value = true
  
  try {
    const data: any = {}
    
    if (exportOptions.value.locations) {
      data.locations = locationStore.getAllLocations()
    }
    
    if (exportOptions.value.routes) {
      data.routes = routeStore.getAllRoutes()
    }
    
    if (exportOptions.value.settings) {
      data.settings = {
        autoSync: autoSyncEnabled.value,
        exportFormat: exportFormat.value
      }
    }
    
    let content = ''
    let filename = ''
    let mimeType = ''
    
    switch (exportFormat.value) {
      case 'json':
        content = JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)
        filename = `mapsxplr-export-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.json`
        mimeType = 'application/json'
        break
        
      case 'gpx':
        content = convertToGPX(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-export-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.gpx`
        mimeType = 'application/gpx+xml'
        break
        
      case 'kml':
        content = convertToKML(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-export-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.kml`
        mimeType = 'application/vnd.google-earth.kml+xml'
        break
        
      case 'csv':
        content = convertToCSV(data)
        filename = `mapsxplr-export-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.csv`
        mimeType = 'text/csv'
        break
    }
    
    // ä¸‹è½½æ–‡ä»¶
    const blob = new Blob([content], { type: mimeType })
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
    const a = document.createElement('a')
    a.href = url
    a.download = filename
    document.body.appendChild(a)
    a.click()
    document.body.removeChild(a)
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url)
    
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'success',
      message: `æ•°æ®å·²å¯¼å‡ºä¸º ${exportFormat.value.toUpperCase()} æ ¼å¼`
    })
    
  } catch (error) {
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'error',
      message: 'å¯¼å‡ºå¤±è´¥: ' + (error as Error).message
    })
  } finally {
    isExporting.value = false
  }
}

// æ ¼å¼è½¬æ¢å‡½æ•°
const convertToGPX = (data: any) => {
  let gpx = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<gpx version="1.1" creator="MAPSXPLR">
`
  
  if (data.locations) {
    data.locations.forEach((location: any) => {
      gpx += `  <wpt lat="${location.lat}" lon="${location.lng}">
`
      gpx += `    <name>${escapeXml(location.name)}</name>
`
      if (location.description) {
        gpx += `    <desc>${escapeXml(location.description)}</desc>
`
      }
      gpx += `    <time>${location.timestamp}</time>
`
      gpx += `  </wpt>
`
    })
  }
  
  if (data.routes) {
    data.routes.forEach((route: any) => {
      gpx += `  <trk>
`
      gpx += `    <name>${escapeXml(route.name)}</name>
`
      gpx += `    <trkseg>
`
      route.points.forEach((point: any) => {
        gpx += `      <trkpt lat="${point.lat}" lon="${point.lng}"></trkpt>
`
      })
      gpx += `    </trkseg>
`
      gpx += `  </trk>
`
    })
  }
  
  gpx += `</gpx>`
  return gpx
}

const convertToKML = (data: any) => {
  let kml = `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<kml xmlns="http://www.opengis.net/kml/2.2">
<Document>
`
  
  if (data.locations) {
    data.locations.forEach((location: any) => {
      kml += `  <Placemark>
`
      kml += `    <name>${escapeXml(location.name)}</name>
`
      if (location.description) {
        kml += `    <description>${escapeXml(location.description)}</description>
`
      }
      kml += `    <Point>
`
      kml += `      <coordinates>${location.lng},${location.lat},0</coordinates>
`
      kml += `    </Point>
`
      kml += `  </Placemark>
`
    })
  }
  
  kml += `</Document>
</kml>`
  return kml
}

const convertToCSV = (data: any) => {
  let csv = 'Type,Name,Description,Latitude,Longitude,Timestamp\n'
  
  if (data.locations) {
    data.locations.forEach((location: any) => {
      csv += `Location,"${location.name}","${location.description || ''}",${location.lat},${location.lng},${location.timestamp}\n`
    })
  }
  
  return csv
}

const escapeXml = (text: string) => {
  return text
    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;')
}

// æ–‡ä»¶é€‰æ‹©å’Œå¯¼å…¥
const triggerFileSelect = () => {
  fileInput.value?.click()
}

const handleFileSelect = (event: Event) => {
  const target = event.target as HTMLInputElement
  if (target.files && target.files[0]) {
    importFile.value = target.files[0]
  }
}

const handleFileDrop = (event: DragEvent) => {
  event.preventDefault()
  if (event.dataTransfer?.files && event.dataTransfer.files[0]) {
    importFile.value = event.dataTransfer.files[0]
  }
}

const importData = async () => {
  if (!importFile.value) return
  
  isImporting.value = true
  
  try {
    const content = await readFileContent(importFile.value)
    const extension = importFile.value.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase()
    
    let data: any = {}
    
    switch (extension) {
      case 'json':
        data = JSON.parse(content)
        break
        
      case 'gpx':
        data = parseGPX(content)
        break
        
      case 'kml':
        data = parseKML(content)
        break
        
      case 'csv':
        data = parseCSV(content)
        break
        
      default:
        throw new Error('ä¸æ”¯æŒçš„æ–‡ä»¶æ ¼å¼')
    }
    
    // å¯¼å…¥æ•°æ®
    if (data.locations) {
      data.locations.forEach((location: any) => {
        locationStore.addLocation({
          ...location,
          id: Date.now().toString() + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)
        })
      })
    }
    
    if (data.routes) {
      data.routes.forEach((route: any) => {
        routeStore.addRoute({
          ...route,
          id: Date.now().toString() + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)
        })
      })
    }
    
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'success',
      message: `æˆåŠŸå¯¼å…¥ ${data.locations?.length || 0} ä¸ªä½ç½®å’Œ ${data.routes?.length || 0} æ¡è·¯çº¿`
    })
    
    importFile.value = null
    if (fileInput.value) {
      fileInput.value.value = ''
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'error',
      message: 'å¯¼å…¥å¤±è´¥: ' + (error as Error).message
    })
  } finally {
    isImporting.value = false
  }
}

// æ–‡ä»¶è§£æå‡½æ•°
const readFileContent = (file: File): Promise<string> => {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const reader = new FileReader()
    reader.onload = (e) => resolve(e.target?.result as string)
    reader.onerror = (e) => reject(new Error('æ–‡ä»¶è¯»å–å¤±è´¥'))
    reader.readAsText(file)
  })
}

const parseGPX = (content: string) => {
  // ç®€åŒ–çš„GPXè§£æ
  const parser = new DOMParser()
  const doc = parser.parseFromString(content, 'text/xml')
  
  const locations: any[] = []
  const waypoints = doc.querySelectorAll('wpt')
  
  waypoints.forEach(wpt => {
    const lat = parseFloat(wpt.getAttribute('lat') || '0')
    const lng = parseFloat(wpt.getAttribute('lon') || '0')
    const name = wpt.querySelector('name')?.textContent || 'æœªå‘½åä½ç½®'
    const description = wpt.querySelector('desc')?.textContent || ''
    const time = wpt.querySelector('time')?.textContent || new Date().toISOString()
    
    locations.push({
      name,
      description,
      lat,
      lng,
      timestamp: time
    })
  })
  
  return { locations }
}

const parseKML = (content: string) => {
  // ç®€åŒ–çš„KMLè§£æ
  const parser = new DOMParser()
  const doc = parser.parseFromString(content, 'text/xml')
  
  const locations: any[] = []
  const placemarks = doc.querySelectorAll('Placemark')
  
  placemarks.forEach(placemark => {
    const name = placemark.querySelector('name')?.textContent || 'æœªå‘½åä½ç½®'
    const description = placemark.querySelector('description')?.textContent || ''
    const coordinates = placemark.querySelector('coordinates')?.textContent?.trim()
    
    if (coordinates) {
      const [lng, lat] = coordinates.split(',').map(Number)
      locations.push({
        name,
        description,
        lat,
        lng,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      })
    }
  })
  
  return { locations }
}

const parseCSV = (content: string) => {
  const lines = content.split('\n')
  const headers = lines[0].split(',')
  const locations: any[] = []
  
  for (let i = 1; i < lines.length; i++) {
    const values = lines[i].split(',')
    if (values.length >= 5 && values[0] === 'Location') {
      locations.push({
        name: values[1].replace(/"/g, ''),
        description: values[2].replace(/"/g, ''),
        lat: parseFloat(values[3]),
        lng: parseFloat(values[4]),
        timestamp: values[5] || new Date().toISOString()
      })
    }
  }
  
  return { locations }
}

// äº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥
const uploadToCloud = async () => {
  isSyncing.value = true
  syncStatus.value = 'syncing'
  
  try {
    // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿäº‘ç«¯ä¸Šä¼ 
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000))
    
    syncStatus.value = 'connected'
    lastSyncTime.value = new Date().toLocaleString('zh-CN')
    
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'success',
      message: 'æ•°æ®å·²æˆåŠŸä¸Šä¼ åˆ°äº‘ç«¯'
    })
    
  } catch (error) {
    syncStatus.value = 'error'
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'error',
      message: 'äº‘ç«¯ä¸Šä¼ å¤±è´¥'
    })
  } finally {
    isSyncing.value = false
  }
}

const downloadFromCloud = async () => {
  isSyncing.value = true
  syncStatus.value = 'syncing'
  
  try {
    // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿäº‘ç«¯ä¸‹è½½
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000))
    
    syncStatus.value = 'connected'
    lastSyncTime.value = new Date().toLocaleString('zh-CN')
    
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'success',
      message: 'æ•°æ®å·²ä»äº‘ç«¯åŒæ­¥'
    })
    
  } catch (error) {
    syncStatus.value = 'error'
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'error',
      message: 'äº‘ç«¯ä¸‹è½½å¤±è´¥'
    })
  } finally {
    isSyncing.value = false
  }
}

const toggleAutoSync = () => {
  autoSyncEnabled.value = !autoSyncEnabled.value
  
  notificationStore.addNotification({
    type: 'info',
    message: `è‡ªåŠ¨åŒæ­¥å·²${autoSyncEnabled.value ? 'å¼€å¯' : 'å…³é—­'}`
  })
}

const getSyncStatusText = () => {
  switch (syncStatus.value) {
    case 'connected': return 'å·²è¿æ¥'
    case 'syncing': return 'åŒæ­¥ä¸­...'
    case 'error': return 'è¿æ¥é”™è¯¯'
    default: return 'æœªè¿æ¥'
  }
}

// å¤‡ä»½ç®¡ç†
const createBackup = async () => {
  isCreatingBackup.value = true
  
  try {
    const data = {
      locations: locationStore.getAllLocations(),
      routes: routeStore.getAllRoutes(),
      settings: {
        autoSync: autoSyncEnabled.value,
        exportFormat: exportFormat.value
      },
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }
    
    const backup = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      name: `å¤‡ä»½_${new Date().toLocaleString('zh-CN').replace(/[/:]/g, '-')}`,
      date: new Date().toISOString(),
      size: new Blob([JSON.stringify(data)]).size,
      data
    }
    
    backups.value.unshift(backup)
    
    // ä¿å­˜åˆ°æœ¬åœ°å­˜å‚¨
    localStorage.setItem('mapsxplr_backups', JSON.stringify(backups.value))
    
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'success',
      message: 'å¤‡ä»½åˆ›å»ºæˆåŠŸ'
    })
    
  } catch (error) {
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'error',
      message: 'å¤‡ä»½åˆ›å»ºå¤±è´¥'
    })
  } finally {
    isCreatingBackup.value = false
  }
}

const restoreBackup = (backup: any) => {
  if (confirm('ç¡®å®šè¦æ¢å¤æ­¤å¤‡ä»½å—ï¼Ÿå½“å‰æ•°æ®å°†è¢«è¦†ç›–ã€‚')) {
    try {
      // æ¸…é™¤å½“å‰æ•°æ®
      locationStore.clearAllLocations()
      routeStore.clearAllRoutes()
      
      // æ¢å¤å¤‡ä»½æ•°æ®
      if (backup.data.locations) {
        backup.data.locations.forEach((location: any) => {
          locationStore.addLocation(location)
        })
      }
      
      if (backup.data.routes) {
        backup.data.routes.forEach((route: any) => {
          routeStore.addRoute(route)
        })
      }
      
      notificationStore.addNotification({
        type: 'success',
        message: 'å¤‡ä»½æ¢å¤æˆåŠŸ'
      })
      
    } catch (error) {
      notificationStore.addNotification({
        type: 'error',
        message: 'å¤‡ä»½æ¢å¤å¤±è´¥'
      })
    }
  }
}

const deleteBackup = (backup: any) => {
  if (confirm('ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤æ­¤å¤‡ä»½å—ï¼Ÿ')) {
    const index = backups.value.findIndex(b => b.id === backup.id)
    if (index !== -1) {
      backups.value.splice(index, 1)
      localStorage.setItem('mapsxplr_backups', JSON.stringify(backups.value))
      
      notificationStore.addNotification({
        type: 'info',
        message: 'å¤‡ä»½å·²åˆ é™¤'
      })
    }
  }
}

const cleanOldBackups = () => {
  const oneWeekAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)
  const oldBackups = backups.value.filter(backup => new Date(backup.date) < oneWeekAgo)
  
  if (oldBackups.length === 0) {
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'info',
      message: 'æ²¡æœ‰éœ€è¦æ¸…ç†çš„æ—§å¤‡ä»½'
    })
    return
  }
  
  if (confirm(`ç¡®å®šè¦åˆ é™¤ ${oldBackups.length} ä¸ªä¸€å‘¨å‰çš„å¤‡ä»½å—ï¼Ÿ`)) {
    backups.value = backups.value.filter(backup => new Date(backup.date) >= oneWeekAgo)
    localStorage.setItem('mapsxplr_backups', JSON.stringify(backups.value))
    
    notificationStore.addNotification({
      type: 'success',
      message: `å·²æ¸…ç† ${oldBackups.length} ä¸ªæ—§å¤‡ä»½`
    })
  }
}

// å·¥å…·å‡½æ•°
const formatFileSize = (bytes: number) => {
  if (bytes === 0) return '0 B'
  const k = 1024
  const sizes = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB']
  const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k))
  return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + ' ' + sizes[i]
}

const formatDate = (dateString: string) => {
  return new Date(dateString).toLocaleString('zh-CN')
}

// ç”Ÿå‘½å‘¨æœŸ
onMounted(() => {
  // åŠ è½½å¤‡ä»½åˆ—è¡¨
  const savedBackups = localStorage.getItem('mapsxplr_backups')
  if (savedBackups) {
    backups.value = JSON.parse(savedBackups)
  }
  
  // åŠ è½½åŒæ­¥è®¾ç½®
  const savedAutoSync = localStorage.getItem('mapsxplr_auto_sync')
  if (savedAutoSync) {
    autoSyncEnabled.value = JSON.parse(savedAutoSync)
  }
  
  const savedLastSync = localStorage.getItem('mapsxplr_last_sync')
  if (savedLastSync) {
    lastSyncTime.value = savedLastSync
  }
})
</script>
